Vālmīki Rāmāyaṇa
 Araṇyakāṇḍa
a praviśya tu mahāraṇyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyam ātmavān
c dadarśa rāmo durdharṣas tāpasāśramamaṇḍalam
a kuśacīraparikṣiptaṃ brāhmyā lakṣmyā samāvṛtam
c yathā pradīptaṃ durdharśaṃ gagane sūryamaṇḍalam
a śaraṇyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ susamṛṣṭājiraṃ sadā
c pūjitaṃ copanṛttaṃ ca nityam apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
a viśālair agniśaraṇaiḥ srugbhāṇḍair ajinaiḥ kuśaiḥ
c samidbhis toyakalaśaiḥ phalamūlaiś ca śobhitam
a āraṇyaiś ca mahāvṛkṣaiḥ puṇyaiḥ svāduphalair vṛtam
c balihomārcitaṃ puṇyaṃ brahmaghoṣanināditam
a puṣpair vanyaiḥ parikṣiptaṃ padminyā ca sapadmayā
c phalamūlāśanair dāntaiś cīrakṛṣṇājināmbaraiḥ
a sūryavaiśvānarābhaiś ca purāṇair munibhir vṛtam
c puṇyaiś a niyatāhāraiḥ śobhitaṃ paramarṣibhiḥ
a tad brahmabhavanaprakhyaṃ brahmaghoṣanināditam
c brahmavidbhir mahābhāgair brāhmaṇair upaśobhitam
a tad dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ śrīmāṃs tāpasāśramamaṇḍalam
c abhyagacchan mahātejā vijyaṃ kṛtvā mahad dhanuḥ
a divyajñānopapannās te rāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā maharṣayaḥ
c abhyagacchaṃs tadā prītā vaidehīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
a te taṃ somam ivodyantaṃ dṛṣṭvā vai dharmacāriṇaḥ
c maṅgalāni prayuñjānāḥ pratyagṛhṇan dṛḍhavratāḥ
a rūpasaṃhananaṃ lakṣmīṃ saukumāryaṃ suveṣatām
c dadṛśur vismitākārā rāmasya vanavāsinaḥ
a vaidehīṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ rāmaṃ netrair animiṣair iva
c āścaryabhūtān dadṛśuḥ sarve te vanacāriṇaḥ
a atrainaṃ hi mahābhāgāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
c atithiṃ parṇaśālāyāṃ rāghavaṃ saṃnyaveśayan
a tato rāmasya satkṛtya vidhinā pāvakopamāḥ
c ājahrus te mahābhāgāḥ salilaṃ dharmacāriṇaḥ
a mūlaṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ vanyam āśramaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
c nivedayītvā dharmajñās tataḥ prāñjalayo 'bruvan
a dharmapālo janasyāsya śaraṇyaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
c pūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca rājā daṇḍadharo guruḥ
a indrasyaiva caturbhāgaḥ prajā rakṣati rāghava
c rājā tasmād vanān bhogān bhuṅkte lokanamaskṛtaḥ
a te vayaṃ bhavatā rakṣyā bhavadviṣayavāsinaḥ
c nagarastho vanastho vā tvaṃ no rājā janeśvaraḥ
a nyastadaṇḍā vayaṃ rājañ jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ
c rakṣitavyās tvayā śaśvad garbhabhūtās tapodhanāḥ
a evam uktvā phalair mūlaiḥ puṣpair vanyaiś ca rāghavam
c anyaiś ca vividhāhāraiḥ salakṣmaṇam apūjayan
a tathānye tāpasāḥ siddhā rāmaṃ vaiśvānaropamāḥ
c nyāyavṛttā yathānyāyaṃ tarpayām āsur īśvaram
a kṛtātithyo 'tha rāmas tu sūryasyodayanaṃ prati
c āmantrya sa munīn sarvān vanam evānvagāhata
a nānāmṛgagaṇākīrṇaṃ śārdūlavṛkasevitam
c dhvastavṛkṣalatāgulmaṃ durdarśa salilāśayam
a niṣkūjanānāśakuni jhillikā gaṇanāditam
c lakṣmaṇānugato rāmo vanamadhyaṃ dadarśa ha
a vanamadhye tu kākutsthas tasmin ghoramṛgāyute
c dadarśa giriśṛṅgābhaṃ puruṣādaṃ mahāsvanam
a gabhīrākṣaṃ mahāvaktraṃ vikaṭaṃ viṣamodaram
c bībhatsaṃ viṣamaṃ dīrghaṃ vikṛtaṃ ghoradarśanam
a vasānaṃ carmavaiyāghraṃ vasārdraṃ rudhirokṣitam
c trāsanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
a trīn siṃhāṃś caturo vyāghrān dvau vṛkau pṛṣatān daśa
c saviṣāṇaṃ vasādigdhaṃ gajasya ca śiro mahat
a avasajyāyase śūle vinadantaṃ mahāsvanam
c sa rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva sītāṃ dṛṣṭvā ca maithilīm
a abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddhaḥ prajāḥ kāla ivāntakaḥ
c sa kṛtvā bhairavaṃ nādaṃ cālayann iva medinīm
a aṅgenādāya vaidehīm apakramya tato 'bravīt
c yuvāṃ jaṭācīradharau sabhāryau kṣīṇajīvitau
a praviṣṭau daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ śaracāpāsidhāriṇau
c kathaṃ tāpasayor vāṃ ca vāsaḥ pramadayā saha
a adharmacāriṇau pāpau kau yuvāṃ munidūṣakau
c ahaṃ vanam idaṃ durgaṃ virāgho nāma rākṣasaḥ
a carāmi sāyudho nityam ṛṣimāṃsāni bhakṣayan
c iyaṃ nārī varārohā mama bharyā bhaviṣyati
e yuvayoḥ pāpayoś cāhaṃ pāsyāmi rudhiraṃ mṛdhe
a tasyaivaṃ bruvato dhṛṣṭaṃ virādhasya durātmanaḥ
c śrutvā sagarvitaṃ vākyaṃ saṃbhrāntā janakātmajā
e sītā prāvepatodvegāt pravāte kadalī yathā
a tāṃ dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ sītāṃ virādhāṅkagatāṃ śubhām
c abravīl lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā
a paśya saumya narendrasya janakasyātmasaṃbhavām
c mama bhāryāṃ śubhācārāṃ virādhāṅke praveśitām
e atyanta sukhasaṃvṛddhāṃ rājaputrīṃ yaśasvinīm
a yad abhipretam asmāsu priyaṃ vara vṛtaṃ ca yat
c kaikeyyās tu susaṃvṛttaṃ kṣipram adyaiva lakṣmaṇa
a yā na tuṣyati rājyena putrārthe dīrghadarśinī
c yayāhaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ hitaḥ prasthāpito vanam
e adyedānīṃ sakāmā sā yā mātā mama madhyamā
a parasparśāt tu vaidehyā na duḥkhataram asti me
c pitur vināśāt saumitre svarājyaharaṇāt tathā
a iti bruvati kākutsthe bāṣpaśokapariplute
c abravīl lakṣmaṇaḥ kruddho ruddho nāga iva śvasan
a anātha iva bhūtānāṃ nāthas tvaṃ vāsavopamaḥ
c mayā preṣyeṇa kākutstha kimarthaṃ paritapsyase
a śareṇa nihatasyādya mayā kruddhena rakṣasaḥ
c virādhasya gatāsor hi mahī pāsyati śoṇitam
a rājyakāme mama krodho bharate yo babhūva ha
c taṃ virādhe vimokṣyāmi vajrī vajram ivācale
a mama bhujabalavegavegitaḥ
patatu śaro 'sya mahān mahorasi
c vyapanayatu tanoś ca jīvitaṃ
patatu tataś ca mahīṃ vighūrṇitaḥ
a athovāca punar vākyaṃ virādhaḥ pūrayan vanam
c ātmānaṃ pṛcchate brūtaṃ kau yuvāṃ kva gamiṣyathaḥ
a tam uvāca tato rāmo rākṣasaṃ jvalitānanam
c pṛcchantaṃ sumahātejā ikṣvākukulam ātmanaḥ
a kṣatriyo vṛttasaṃpannau viddhi nau vanagocarau
c tvāṃ tu veditum icchāvaḥ kas tvaṃ carasi daṇḍakān
a tam uvāca virādhas tu rāmaṃ satyaparākramam
c hanta vakṣyāmi te rājan nibodha mama rāghava
a putraḥ kila jayasyāhaṃ mātā mama śatahradā
c virādha iti mām āhuḥ pṛthivyāṃ sarvarākṣasāḥ
a tapasā cāpi me prāptā brahmaṇo hi prasādajā
c śastreṇāvadhyatā loke 'cchedyābhedyatvam eva ca
a utsṛjya pramadām enām anapekṣau yathāgatam
c tvaramāṇau pālayethāṃ na vāṃ jīvitam ādade
a taṃ rāmaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ kopasaṃraktalocanaḥ
c rākṣasaṃ vikṛtākāraṃ virādhaṃ pāpacetasaṃ
a kṣudra dhik tvāṃ tu hīnārthaṃ mṛtyum anveṣase dhruvam
c raṇe saṃprāpsyase tiṣṭha na me jīvan gamiṣyasi
a tataḥ sajyaṃ dhanuḥ kṛtvā rāmaḥ suniśitāñ śarān
c suśīghram abhisaṃdhāya rākṣasaṃ nijaghāna ha
a dhanuṣā jyāguṇavatā saptabāṇān mumoca ha
c rukmapuṅkhān mahāvegān suparṇānilatulyagān
a te śarīraṃ virādhasya bhittvā barhiṇavāsasaḥ
c nipetuḥ śoṇitādigdhā dharaṇyāṃ pāvakopamāḥ
a sa vinadya mahānādaṃ śūlaṃ śakradhvajopamam
c pragṛhyāśobhata tadā vyāttānana ivāntakaḥ
a tac chūlaṃ vajrasaṃkāśaṃ gagane jvalanopamam
c dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ ciccheda rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a tasya raudrasya saumitrir bāhuṃ savyaṃ babhañja ha
c rāmas tu dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ tarasā tasya rakṣasaḥ
a sa bhagnabāhuḥ saṃvigno nipapātāśu rākṣasaḥ
c dharaṇyāṃ meghasaṃkāśo vajrabhinna ivācalaḥ
e idaṃ provāca kākutsthaṃ virādhaḥ puruṣarṣabham
a kausalyā suprajās tāta rāmas tvaṃ vidito mayā
c vaidehī ca mahābhāgā lakṣmaṇaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
a abhiśāpād ahaṃ ghorāṃ praviṣṭo rākṣasīṃ tanum
c tumburur nāma gandharvaḥ śapto vaiśvaraṇena hi
a prasādyamānaś ca mayā so 'bravīn māṃ mahāyaśāḥ
c yadā dāśarathī rāmas tvāṃ vadhiṣyati saṃyuge
a tadā prakṛtim āpanno bhavān svargaṃ gamiṣyati
c iti vaiśravaṇo rājā rambhāsaktam uvāca ha
a anupasthīyamāno māṃ saṃkruddho vyajahāra ha
c tava prasādān mukto 'ham abhiśāpāt sudāruṇāt
e bhavanaṃ svaṃ gamiṣyāmi svasti vo 'stu paraṃtapa
a ito vasati dharmātmā śarabhaṅgaḥ pratāpavān
c adhyardhayojane tāta maharṣiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaḥ
a taṃ kṣipram abhigaccha tvaṃ sa te śreyo vidhāsyati
c avaṭe cāpi māṃ rāma nikṣipya kuśalī vraja
a rakṣasāṃ gatasattvānām eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
c avaṭe ye nidhīyante teṣāṃ lokāḥ sanātanāḥ
a evam uktvā tu kākutsthaṃ virādhaḥ śarapīḍitaḥ
c babhūva svargasaṃprāpto nyastadeho mahābalaḥ
a taṃ muktakaṇṭham utkṣipya śaṅkukarṇaṃ mahāsvanam
c virādhaṃ prākṣipac chvabhre nadantaṃ bhairavasvanam
a tatas tu tau kāñcanacitrakārmukau
nihatya rakṣaḥ parigṛhya maithilīm
c vijahratus tau muditau mahāvane
divi sthitau candradivākarāv iva
a hatvā tu taṃ bhīmabalaṃ virādhaṃ rākṣasaṃ vane
c tataḥ sītāṃ pariṣvajya samāśvāsya ca vīryavān
e abravīl lakṣmaṇāṃ rāmo bhrātaraṃ dīptatejasaṃ
a kaṣṭaṃ vanam idaṃ durgaṃ na ca smo vanagocarāḥ
c abhigacchāmahe śīghraṃ śarabhaṅgaṃ tapodhanam
a āśramaṃ śarabhaṅgasya rāghavo 'bhijagāma ha
a tasya devaprabhāvasya tapasā bhāvitātmanaḥ
c samīpe śarabhaṅgasya dadarśa mahad adbhutam
a vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā sūryavaiśvānaropamam
c asaṃspṛśantaṃ vasudhāṃ dadarśa vibudheśvaram
a suprabhābharaṇaṃ devaṃ virajo 'mbaradhāriṇam
c tadvidhair eva bahubhiḥ pūjyamānaṃ mahātmabhiḥ
a haribhir vājibhir yuktam antarikṣagataṃ ratham
c dadarśādūratas tasya taruṇādityasaṃnibham
a pāṇḍurābhraghanaprakhyaṃ candramaṇḍalasaṃnibham
c apaśyad vimalaṃ chatraṃ citramālyopaśobhitam
a cāmaravyajane cāgrye rukmadaṇḍe mahādhane
c gṛhīte vananārībhyāṃ dhūyamāne ca mūrdhani
a gandharvāmarasiddhāś ca bahavaḥ paramarṣayaḥ
c antarikṣagataṃ devaṃ vāgbhir agryābhir īḍire
a dṛṣṭvā śatakratuṃ tatra rāmo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
c ye hayāḥ puruhūtasya purā śakrasya naḥ śrutāḥ
e antarikṣagatā divyās ta ime harayo dhruvam
a ime ca puruṣavyāghra ye tiṣṭhanty abhito ratham
c śataṃ śataṃ kuṇḍalino yuvānaḥ khaḍgapāṇayaḥ
a urodeśeṣu sarveṣāṃ hārā jvalanasaṃnibhāḥ
c rūpaṃ bibhrati saumitre pañcaviṃśativārṣikam
a etad dhi kila devānāṃ vayo bhavati nityadā
c yatheme puruṣavyāghrā dṛśyante priyadarśanāḥ
a ihaiva saha vaidehyā muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭha lakṣmaṇa
c yāvaj janāmy ahaṃ vyaktaṃ ka eṣa dyutimān rathe
a tam evam uktvā saumitrim ihaiva sthīyatām iti
c abhicakrāma kākutsthaḥ śarabhaṅgāśramaṃ prati
a tataḥ samabhigacchantaṃ prekṣya rāmaṃ śacīpatiḥ
c śarabhaṅgam anujñāpya vibudhān idam abravīt
a ihopayāty asau rāmo yāvan māṃ nābhibhāṣate
c niṣṭhāṃ nayata tāvat tu tato māṃ draṣṭum arhati
a jitavantaṃ kṛtārthaṃ ca draṣṭāham acirād imam
c karma hy anena kartavyaṃ mahad anyaiḥ suduṣkaram
a iti vajrī tam āmantrya mānayitvā ca tāpasaṃ
c rathena hariyuktena yayau divam ariṃdamaḥ
a prayāte tu sahasrākṣe rāghavaḥ saparicchadaḥ
c agnihotram upāsīnaṃ śarabhaṅgam upāgamat
a tasya pādau ca saṃgṛhya rāmaḥ sītā ca lakṣmaṇaḥ
c niṣedus tadanujñātā labdhavāsā nimantritāḥ
a tataḥ śakropayānaṃ tu paryapṛcchat sa rāghavaḥ
c śarabhaṅgaś ca tat sarvaṃ rāghavāya nyavedayat
a mām eṣa varado rāma brahmalokaṃ ninīṣati
c jitam ugreṇa tapasā duṣprāpam akṛtātmabhiḥ
a ahaṃ jñātvā naravyāghra vartamānam adūrataḥ
c brahmalokaṃ na gacchāmi tvām adṛṣṭvā priyātithim
a samāgamya gamiṣyāmi tridivaṃ devasevitam
c akṣayā naraśārdūla jitā lokā mayā śubhāḥ
e brāhmyāś ca nākapṛṣṭhyāś ca pratigṛhṇīṣva māmakān
a evam ukto naravyāghraḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
c ṛṣiṇā śarabhaṅgena rāghavo vākyam abravīt
a aham evāhariṣyāmi sarvāṃl lokān mahāmune
c āvāsaṃ tv aham icchāmi pradiṣṭam iha kānane
a rāghaveṇaivam uktas tu śakratulyabalena vai
c śarabhaṅgo mahāprājñaḥ punar evābravīd vacaḥ
a sutīkṣṇam abhigaccha tvaṃ śucau deśe tapasvinam
c ramaṇīye vanoddeśe sa te vāsaṃ vidhāsyati
a eṣa panthā naravyāghra muhūrtaṃ paśya tāta mām
c yāvaj jahāmi gātrāṇi jīrṇaṃ tvacam ivoragaḥ
a tato 'gniṃ sa samādhāya hutvā cājyena mantravit
c śarabhaṅgo mahātejāḥ praviveśa hutāśanam
a tasya romāṇi keśāṃś ca dadāhāgnir mahātmanaḥ
c jīrṇaṃ tvacaṃ tathāsthīni yac ca māṃsaṃ ca śoṇitam
a sa ca pāvakasaṃkāśaḥ kumāraḥ samapadyata
c utthāyāgnicayāt tasmāc charabhaṅgo vyarocata
a sa lokān āhitāgnīnām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
c devānāṃ ca vyatikramya brahmalokaṃ vyarohata
a sa puṇyakarmā bhuvane dvijarṣabhaḥ
pitāmahaṃ sānucaraṃ dadarśa ha
c pitāmahaś cāpi samīkṣya taṃ dvijaṃ
nananda susvāgatam ity uvāca ha
a śarabhaṅge divaṃ prāpte munisaṃghāḥ samāgatāḥ
c abhyagacchanta kākutsthaṃ rāmaṃ jvalitatejasaṃ
a vaikhānasā vālakhilyāḥ saṃprakṣālā marīcipāḥ
c aśmakuṭṭāś ca bahavaḥ patrāhārāś ca tāpasāḥ
a dantolūkhalinaś caiva tathaivonmajjakāḥ pare
c munayaḥ salilāhārā vāyubhakṣās tathāpare
a ākāśanilayāś caiva tathā sthaṇḍilaśāyinaḥ
c tathordhvavāsino dāntās tathārdrapaṭavāsasaḥ
a sajapāś ca taponityās tathā pañcatapo'nvitāḥ
c sarve brāhmyā śriyā juṣṭā dṛḍhayogasamāhitāḥ
e śarabhaṅgāśrame rāmam abhijagmuś ca tāpasāḥ
a abhigamya ca dharmajñā rāmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varam
c ūcuḥ paramadharmajñam ṛṣisaṃghāḥ samāhitāḥ
a tvam ikṣvākukulasyāsya pṛthivyāś ca mahārathaḥ
c pradhānaś cāsi nāthaś ca devānāṃ maghavān iva
a viśrutas triṣu lokeṣu yaśasā vikrameṇa ca
c pitṛvratatvaṃ satyaṃ ca tvayi dharmaś ca puṣkalaḥ
a tvām āsādya mahātmānaṃ dharmajñaṃ dharmavatsalam
c arthitvān nātha vakṣyāmas tac ca naḥ kṣantum arhasi
a adhārmas tu mahāṃs tāta bhavet tasya mahīpateḥ
c yo hared baliṣaḍbhāgaṃ na ca rakṣati putravat
a yuñjānaḥ svān iva prāṇān prāṇair iṣṭān sutān iva
c nityayuktaḥ sadā rakṣan sarvān viṣayavāsinaḥ
a prāpnoti śāśvatīṃ rāma kīrtiṃ sa bahuvārṣikīm
c brahmaṇaḥ sthānam āsādya tatra cāpi mahīyate
a yat karoti paraṃ dharmaṃ munir mūlaphalāśanaḥ
c tatra rājñaś caturbhāgaḥ prajā dharmeṇa rakṣataḥ
a so 'yaṃ brāhmaṇabhūyiṣṭho vānaprasthagaṇo mahān
c tvan nātho 'nāthavad rāma rākṣasair vadhyate bhṛśam
a ehi paśya śarīrāṇi munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām
c hatānāṃ rākṣasair ghorair bahūnāṃ bahudhā vane
a pampānadīnivāsānām anumandākinīm api
c citrakūṭālayānāṃ ca kriyate kadanaṃ mahat
a evaṃ vayaṃ na mṛṣyāmo viprakāraṃ tapasvinam
c kriyamāṇaṃ vane ghoraṃ rakṣobhir bhīmakarmabhiḥ
a tatas tvāṃ śaraṇārthaṃ ca śaraṇyaṃ samupasthitāḥ
c paripālaya no rāma vadhyamānān niśācaraiḥ
a etac chrutvā tu kākutsthas tāpasānāṃ tapasvinām
c idaṃ provāca dharmātmā sarvān eva tapasvinaḥ
e naivam arhatha māṃ vaktum ājñāpyo 'haṃ tapasvinam
a bhavatām arthasiddhyartham āgato 'haṃ yadṛcchayā
c tasya me 'yaṃ vane vāso bhaviṣyati mahāphalaḥ
e tapasvināṃ raṇe śatrūn hantum icchāmi rākṣasān
a dattvā varaṃ cāpi tapodhanānāṃ
dharme dhṛtātmā sahalakṣmaṇena
c tapodhanaiś cāpi sahārya vṛttaḥ
sutīṣkṇam evābhijagāma vīraḥ
a rāmas tu sahito bhrātrā sītayā ca paraṃtapaḥ
c sutīkṣṇasyāśramapadaṃ jagāma saha tair dvijaiḥ
a sa gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ nadīs tīrtva bahūdakāḥ
c dadarśa vipulaṃ śailaṃ mahāmegham ivonnatam
a tatas tad ikṣvākuvarau satataṃ vividhair drumaiḥ
c kānanaṃ tau viviśatuḥ sītayā saha rāghavau
a praviṣṭas tu vanaṃ ghoraṃ bahupuṣpaphaladrumam
c dadarśāśramam ekānte cīramālāpariṣkṛtam
a tatra tāpasam āsīnaṃ malapaṅkajaṭādharam
c rāmaḥ sutīkṣṇaṃ vidhivat tapovṛddham abhāṣata
a rāmo 'ham asmi bhagavan bhavantaṃ draṣṭum āgataḥ
c tan mābhivada dharmajña maharṣe satyavikrama
a sa nirīkṣya tato vīraṃ rāmaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varam
c samāśliṣya ca bāhubhyām idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a svāgataṃ khalu te vīra rāma dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
c āśramo 'yaṃ tvayākrāntaḥ sanātha iva sāmpratam
a pratīkṣamāṇas tvām eva nārohe 'haṃ mahāyaśaḥ
c devalokam ito vīra dehaṃ tyaktvā mahītale
a citrakūṭam upādāya rājyabhraṣṭo 'si me śrutaḥ
c ihopayātaḥ kākutstho devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ
e sarvāṃl lokāñ jitān āha mama puṇyena karmaṇā
a teṣu devarṣijuṣṭeṣu jiteṣu tapasā mayā
c matprasādāt sabhāryas tvaṃ viharasva salakṣmaṇaḥ
a tam ugratapasaṃ dīptaṃ maharṣiṃ satyavādinam
c pratyuvācātmavān rāmo brahmāṇam iva vāsavaḥ
a aham evāhariṣyāmi svayaṃ lokān mahāmune
c āvāsaṃ tv aham icchāmi pradiṣṭam iha kānane
a bhavān sarvatra kuśalaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
c ākhyātaḥ śarabhaṅgena gautamena mahātmanā
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa maharṣir lokaviśrutaḥ
c abravīn madhuraṃ vākyaṃ harṣeṇa mahatāplutaḥ
a ayam evāśramo rāma guṇavān ramyatām iha
c ṛṣisaṃghānucaritaḥ sadā mūlaphalair yutaḥ
a imam āśramam āgamya mṛgasaṃghā mahāyaśāḥ
c aṭitvā pratigacchanti lobhayitvākutobhayāḥ
a tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya maharṣer lakṣmaṇāgrajaḥ
c uvāca vacanaṃ dhīro vikṛṣya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ
a tān ahaṃ sumahābhāga mṛgasaṃghān samāgatān
c hanyāṃ niśitadhāreṇa śareṇāśanivarcasā
a bhavāṃs tatrābhiṣajyeta kiṃ syāt kṛcchrataraṃ tataḥ
c etasminn āśrame vāsaṃ ciraṃ tu na samarthaye
a tam evam uktvā varadaṃ rāmaḥ saṃdhyām upāgamat
c anvāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ tatra vāsam akalpayat
a tataḥ śubhaṃ tāpasabhojyam annaṃ
svayaṃ sutīkṣṇaḥ puruṣarṣabhābhyām
c tābhyāṃ susatkṛtya dadau mahātmā
saṃdhyānivṛttau rajanīṃ samīkṣya
a rāmas tu sahasaumitriḥ sutīkṣṇenābhipūjitaḥ
c pariṇamya niśāṃ tatra prabhāte pratyabudhyata
a utthāya tu yathākālaṃ rāghavaḥ saha sītayā
c upāspṛśat suśītena jalenotpalagandhinā
a atha te 'gniṃ surāṃś caiva vaidehī rāmalakṣmaṇau
c kālyaṃ vidhivad abhyarcya tapasviśaraṇe vane
a udayanntaṃ dinakaraṃ dṛṣṭvā vigatakalmaṣāḥ
c sutīkṣṇam abhigamyedaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vacanam abruvan
a sukhoṣitāḥ sma bhagavaṃs tvayā pūjyena pūjitāḥ
c āpṛcchāmaḥ prayāsyāmo munayas tvarayanti naḥ
a tvarāmahe vayaṃ draṣṭuṃ kṛtsnam āśramamaṇḍalam
c ṛṣīṇāṃ puṇyaśīlānāṃ daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinām
a abhyanujñātum icchāmaḥ sahaibhir munipuṅgavaiḥ
c dharmanityais tapodāntair viśikhair iva pāvakaiḥ
a aviṣahyātapo yāvat sūryo nātivirājite
c amārgeṇāgatāṃ lakṣmīṃ prāpyevānvayavarjitaḥ
a tāvad icchāmahe gantum ity uktvā caraṇau muneḥ
c vavande sahasaumitriḥ sītayā saha rāghavaḥ
a tau saṃspṛśantau caraṇāv utthāpya munipuṃgavaḥ
c gāḍham āliṅgya sasneham idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a ariṣṭaṃ gaccha panthānaṃ rāma saumitriṇā saha
c sītayā cānayā sārdhaṃ chāyayevānuvṛttayā
a paśyāśramapadaṃ ramyaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinām
c eṣāṃ tapasvināṃ vīra tapasā bhāvitātmanām
a suprājyaphalamūlāni puṣpitāni vanāni ca
c praśāntamṛgayūthāni śāntapakṣigaṇāni ca
a phullapaṅkajaṣaḍāni prasannasalilāni ca
c kāraṇḍavavikīrṇāni taṭākāni sarāṃsi ca
a drakṣyase dṛṣṭiramyāṇi giriprasravaṇāni ca
c ramaṇīyāny araṇyāni mayūrābhirutāni ca
a gamyatāṃ vatsa saumitre bhavān api ca gacchatu
c āgantavyaṃ ca te dṛṣṭvā punar evāśramaṃ mama
a evam uktas tathety uktvā kākutsthaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c pradakṣiṇaṃ muniṃ kṛtā prasthātum upacakrame
a tataḥ śubhatare tūṇī dhanuṣī cāyatekṣaṇā
c dadau sītā tayor bhrātroḥ khaḍgau ca vimalau tataḥ
a ābadhya ca śubhe tūṇī cāpe cādāya sasvane
c niṣkrāntāv āśramād gantum ubhau tau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a sutīkṣṇenābhyanujñātaṃ prasthitaṃ raghunandanam
c vaidehī snigdhayā vācā bhartāram idam abravīt
a ayaṃ dharmaḥ susūkṣmeṇa vidhinā prāpyate mahān
c nivṛttena ca śakyo 'yaṃ vyasanāt kāmajād iha
a trīṇy eva vyasanāny atra kāmajāni bhavanty uta
c mithyā vākyaṃ paramakaṃ tasmād gurutarāv ubhau
e paradārābhigamanaṃ vinā vairaṃ ca raudratā
a mithyāvākyaṃ na te bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati rāghava
c kuto 'bhilaṣaṇaṃ strīṇāṃ pareṣāṃ dharmanāśanam
a tac ca sarvaṃ mahābāho śakyaṃ voḍhuṃ jitendriyaiḥ
c tava vaśyendriyatvaṃ ca jānāmi śubhadarśana
a tṛtīyaṃ yad idaṃ raudraṃ paraprāṇābhihiṃsanam
c nirvairaṃ kriyate mohāt tac ca te samupasthitam
a pratijñātas tvayā vīra daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinām
c ṛṣīṇāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya vadhaḥ saṃyati rakṣasām
a etannimittaṃ ca vanaṃ daṇḍakā iti viśrutam
c prasthitas tvaṃ saha bhrātrā dhṛtabāṇaśarāsanaḥ
a tatas tvāṃ prasthitaṃ dṛṣṭvā mama cintākulaṃ manaḥ
c tvad vṛttaṃ cintayantyā vai bhaven niḥśreyasaṃ hitam
a na hi me rocate vīra gamanaṃ daṇḍakān prati
c kāraṇaṃ tatra vakṣyāmi vadantyāḥ śrūyatāṃ mama
a tvaṃ hi bāṇadhanuṣpāṇir bhrātrā saha vanaṃ gataḥ
c dṛṣṭvā vanacarān sarvān kaccit kuryāḥ śaravyayam
a kṣatriyāṇām iha dhanur hutāśasyendhanāni ca
c samīpataḥ sthitaṃ tejobalam ucchrayate bhṛśam
a purā kila mahābāho tapasvī satyavāk śuciḥ
c kasmiṃś cid abhavat puṇye vane ratamṛgadvije
a tasyaiva tapaso vighnaṃ kartum indraḥ śacīpatiḥ
c khaḍgapāṇir athāgacchad āśramaṃ bhaṭa rūpadhṛk
a tasmiṃs tad āśramapade nihitaḥ khaḍga uttamaḥ
c sa nyāsavidhinā dattaḥ puṇye tapasi tiṣṭhataḥ
a sa tac chastram anuprāpya nyāsarakṣaṇatatparaḥ
c vane tu vicaraty eva rakṣan pratyayam ātmanaḥ
a yatra gacchaty upādātuṃ mūlāni ca phalāni ca
c na vinā yāti taṃ khaḍgaṃ nyāsarakṣaṇatatparaḥ
a nityaṃ śastraṃ parivahan krameṇa sa tapodhanaḥ
c cakāra raudrīṃ svāṃ buddhiṃ tyaktvā tapasi niścayam
a tataḥ sa raudrābhirataḥ pramatto 'dharmakarṣitaḥ
c tasya śastrasya saṃvāsāj jagāma narakaṃ muniḥ
a snehāc ca bahumānāc ca smāraye tvāṃ na śikṣaye
c na kathaṃ cana sā kāryā hṛhītadhanuṣā tvayā
a buddhir vairaṃ vinā hantuṃ rākṣasān daṇḍakāśritān
c aparādhaṃ vinā hantuṃ lokān vīra na kāmaye
a kṣatriyāṇāṃ tu vīrāṇāṃ vaneṣu niyatātmanām
c dhanuṣā kāryam etāvad ārtānām abhirakṣaṇam
a kva ca śastraṃ kva ca vanaṃ kva ca kṣātraṃ tapaḥ kva ca
c vyāviddham idam asmābhir deśadharmas tu pūjyatām
a tad āryakaluṣā buddhir jāyate śastrasevanāt
c punar gatvā tv ayodhyāyāṃ kṣatradharmaṃ cariṣyasi
a akṣayā tu bhavet prītiḥ śvaśrū śvaśurayor mama
c yadi rājyaṃ hi saṃnyasya bhaves tvaṃ nirato muniḥ
a dharmād arthaḥ prabhavati dharmāt prabhavate sukham
c dharmeṇa labhate sarvaṃ dharmasāram idaṃ jagat
a ātmānaṃ niyamais tais taiḥ karṣayitvā prayatnataḥ
c prāpyate nipuṇair dharmo na sukhāl labhyate sukham
a nityaṃ śucimatiḥ saumya cara dharmaṃ tapovane
c sarvaṃ hi viditaṃ tubhyaṃ trailokyam api tattvataḥ
a strīcāpalād etad udāhṛtaṃ me
dharmaṃ ca vaktuṃ tava kaḥ samarthaḥ
c vicārya buddhyā tu sahānujena
yad rocate tat kuru mācireṇa
a vākyam etat tu vaidehyā vyāhṛtaṃ bhartṛbhaktayā
c śrutvā dharme sthito rāmaḥ pratyuvācātha maithilīm
a hitam uktaṃ tvayā devi snigdhayā sadṛśaṃ vacaḥ
c kulaṃ vyapadiśantyā ca dharmajñe janakātmaje
a kiṃ tu vakṣyāmy ahaṃ devi tvayaivoktam idaṃ vacaḥ
c kṣatriyair dhāryate cāpo nārtaśabdo bhaved iti
a te cārtā daṇḍakāraṇye munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
c māṃ sīte svayam āgamya śaraṇyāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
a vasanto dharmaniratā vane mūlaphalāśanāḥ
c na labhante sukhaṃ bhītā rākṣasaiḥ krūrakarmabhiḥ
a kāle kāle ca niratā niyamair vividhair vane
c bhakṣyante rākṣasair bhīmair naramāṃsopajīvibhiḥ
a te bhakṣyamāṇā munayo daṇḍakāraṇyavāsinaḥ
c asmān abhyavapadyeti mām ūcur dvijasattamāḥ
a mayā tu vacanaṃ śrutvā teṣām evaṃ mukhāc cyutam
c kṛtvā caraṇaśuśrūṣāṃ vākyam etad udāhṛtam
a prasīdantu bhavanto me hrīr eṣā hi mamātulā
c yadīdṛśair ahaṃ viprair upastheyair upasthitaḥ
e kiṃ karomīti ca mayā vyāhṛtaṃ dvijasaṃnidhau
a sarvair eva samāgamya vāg iyaṃ samudāhṛtā
c rākṣasair daṇḍakāraṇye bahubhiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ
e arditāḥ sma bhṛśaṃ rāma bhavān nas trātum arhati
a homakāle tu saṃprāpte parvakāleṣu cānagha
c dharṣayanti sma durdharṣā rākṣasāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
a rākṣasair dharṣitānāṃ ca tāpasānāṃ tapasvinām
c gatiṃ mṛgayamāṇānāṃ bhavān naḥ paramā gatiḥ
a kāmaṃ tapaḥ prabhāvena śaktā hantuṃ niśācarān
c cirārjitaṃ tu necchāmas tapaḥ khaṇḍayituṃ vayam
a bahuvighnaṃ taponityaṃ duścaraṃ caiva rāghava
c tena śāpaṃ na muñcāmo bhakṣyamāṇāś ca rākṣasaiḥ
a tad ardyamānān rakṣobhir daṇḍakāraṇyavāsibhiḥ
c rakṣanas tvaṃ saha bhrātrā tvannāthā hi vayaṃ vane
a mayā caitad vacaḥ śrutvā kārtsnyena paripālanam
c ṛṣīṇāṃ daṇḍakāraṇye saṃśrutaṃ janakātmaje
a saṃśrutya ca na śakṣyāmi jīvamānaḥ pratiśravam
c munīnām anyathā kartuṃ satyam iṣṭaṃ hi me sadā
a apy ahaṃ jīvitaṃ jahyāṃ tvāṃ vā sīte salakṣmaṇām
c na tu pratijñāṃ saṃśrutya brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ
a tad avaśyaṃ mayā kāryam ṛṣīṇāṃ paripālanam
c anuktenāpi vaidehi pratijñāya tu kiṃ punaḥ
a mama snehāc ca sauhārdād idam uktaṃ tvayā vacaḥ
c parituṣṭo 'smy ahaṃ sīte na hy aniṣṭo 'nuśiṣyate
e sadṛśaṃ cānurūpaṃ ca kulasya tava śobhane
a ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ mahātmā
sītāṃ priyāṃ maithila rājaputrīm
c rāmo dhanuṣmān sahalakṣmaṇena
jagāma ramyāṇi tapovanāni
a agrataḥ prayayau rāmaḥ sītā madhye sumadhyamā
c pṛṣṭhatas tu dhanuṣpāṇir lakṣmaṇo 'nujagāma ha
a tau paśyamānau vividhāñ śailaprasthān vanāni ca
c nadīś ca vividhā ramyā jagmatuḥ saha sītayā
a sārasāṃś cakravākāṃś ca nadīpulinacāriṇaḥ
c sarāṃsi ca sapadmāni yutāni jalajaiḥ khagaiḥ
a yūthabaddhāṃś ca pṛṣatān madonmattān viṣāṇinaḥ
c mahiṣāṃś ca varāhāṃś ca gajāṃś ca drumavairiṇaḥ
a te gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ lambamāne divākare
c dadṛśuḥ sahitā ramyaṃ taṭākaṃ yojanāyatam
a padmapuṣkarasaṃbādhaṃ gajayūthair alaṃkṛtam
c sārasair haṃsakādambaiḥ saṃkulaṃ jalacāribhiḥ
a prasannasalile ramyatasmin sarasi śuśruve
c gītavāditranirghoṣo na tu kaś cana dṛśyate
a tataḥ kautūhalād rāmo lakṣmaṇaś ca mahārathaḥ
c muniṃ dharmabhṛtaṃ nāma praṣṭuṃ samupacakrame
a idam atyadbhutaṃ śrutvā sarveṣāṃ no mahāmune
c kautūhalaṃ mahaj jātaṃ kim idaṃ sādhu kathyatām
a tenaivam ukto dharmātmā rāghaveṇa munis tadā
c prabhāvaṃ sarasaḥ kṛtsnam ākhyātum upacakrame
a idaṃ pañcāpsaro nāma taṭākaṃ sārvakālikam
c nirmitaṃ tapasā rāma muninā māṇḍakarṇinā
a sa hi tepe tapas tīvraṃ māṇḍakarṇir mahāmuniḥ
c daśavarṣasahasrāṇi vāyubhakṣo jalāśraya
a tataḥ pravyathitāḥ sarve devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ
c abruvan vacanaṃ sarve paraspara samāgatāḥ
e asmakaṃ kasya cit sthānam eṣa prārthayate muniḥ
a tataḥ kartuṃ tapovighnaṃ sarvair devair niyojitāḥ
c pradhānāpsarasaḥ pañcavidyuccalitavarcasaḥ
a apsarobhis tatas tābhir munir dṛṣṭaparāvaraḥ
c nīto madanavaśyatvaṃ surāṇāṃ kāryasiddhaye
a tāś caivāpsarasaḥ pañcamuneḥ patnītvam āgatāḥ
c taṭāke nirmitaṃ tāsām asminn antarhitaṃ gṛham
a tatraivāpsarasaḥ pañcanivasantyo yathāsukham
c ramayanti tapoyogān muniṃ yauvanam āsthitam
a tāsāṃ saṃkrīḍamānānām eṣa vāditraniḥsvanaḥ
c śrūyate bhūṣaṇonmiśro gītaśabdo manoharaḥ
a āścaryam iti tasyaitad vacanaṃ bhāvitātmanaḥ
c rāghavaḥ pratijagrāha saha bhrātrā mahāyaśāḥ
a evaṃ kathayamānasya dadarśāśramamaṇḍalam
c kuśacīraparikṣiptaṃ nānāvṛkṣasamāvṛtam
a praviśya saha vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca rāghavaḥ
c tadā tasmin sa kākutsthaḥ śrīmaty āśramamaṇḍale
a uṣitvā susukhaṃ tatra pūrjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
c jagāma cāśramāṃs teṣāṃ paryāyeṇa tapasvinām
a yeṣām uṣitavān pūrvaṃ sakāśe sa mahāstravit
c kva cit paridaśān māsān ekaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ kva cit
a kva cic ca caturo māsān pañcaṣaṭ cāparān kva cit
c aparatrādhikān māsān adhyardham adhikaṃ kva cit
a trīn māsān aṣṭamāsāṃś ca rāghavo nyavasat sukham
c tathā saṃvasatas tasya munīnām āśrameṣu vai
e ramataś cānukulyena yayuḥ saṃvatsarā daśa
a parisṛtya ca dharmajño rāghavaḥ saha sītayā
c sutīkṣṇasyāśramaṃ śrīmān punar evājagāma ha
a sa tam āśramam āgamya munibhiḥ pratipūjitaḥ
c tatrāpi nyavasad rāmaḥ kaṃ cit kālam ariṃdamaḥ
a athāśramastho vinayāt kadā cit taṃ mahāmunim
c upāsīnaḥ sa kākutsthaḥ sutīkṣṇam idam abravīt
a asminn araṇye bhagavann agastyo munisattamaḥ
c vasatīti mayā nityaṃ kathāḥ kathayatāṃ śrutam
a na tu jānāmi taṃ deśaṃ vanasyāsya mahattayā
c kutrāśramapadaṃ puṇyaṃ maharṣes tasya dhīmataḥ
a prasādāt tatra bhavataḥ sānujaḥ saha sītayā
c agastyam abhigaccheyam abhivādayituṃ munim
a manoratho mahān eṣa hṛdi saṃparivartate
c yad ahaṃ taṃ munivaraṃ śuśrūṣeyam api svayam
a iti rāmasya sa muniḥ śrutvā dharmātmano vacaḥ
c sutīkṣṇaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ prīto daśarathātmajam
a aham apy etad eva tvāṃ vaktukāmaḥ salakṣmaṇam
c agastyam abhigaccheti sītayā saha rāghava
a diṣṭyā tv idānīm arthe 'smin svayam eva bravīṣi mām
c aham ākhyāsi te vatsa yatrāgastyo mahāmuniḥ
a yojanāny āśramāt tāta yāhi catvāri vai tataḥ
c dakṣiṇena mahāñ śrīmān agastyabhrātur āśramaḥ
a sthalaprāye vanoddeśe pippalīvanaśobhite
c bahupuṣpaphale ramye nānāśakuninādite
a padminyo vividhās tatra prasannasalilāḥ śivāḥ
c haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇāś cakravākopaśobhitāḥ
a tatraikāṃ rajanīm uṣya prabhāte rāma gamyatām
c dakṣiṇāṃ diśam āsthāya vanakhaṇḍasya pārśvataḥ
a tatrāgastyāśramapadaṃ gatvā yojanam antaram
c ramaṇīye vanoddeśe bahupādapa saṃvṛte
e raṃsyate tatra vaidehī lakṣmaṇaś ca tvayā saha
a sa hi ramyo vanoddeśo bahupādapasaṃkulaḥ
c yadi buddhiḥ kṛtā draṣṭum agastyaṃ taṃ mahāmunim
e adyaiva gamane buddhiṃ rocayasva mahāyaśaḥ
a iti rāmo muneḥ śrutvā saha bhrātrābhivādya ca
c pratasthe 'gastyam uddiśya sānujaḥ saha sītayā
a paśyan vanāni citrāṇi parvapāṃś cābhrasaṃnibhān
c sarāṃsi saritaś caiva pathi mārgavaśānugāḥ
a sutīkṣṇenopadiṣṭena gatvā tena pathā sukham
c idaṃ paramasaṃhṛṣṭo vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇam abravīt
a etad evāśramapadaṃ nūnaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ
c agastyasya muner bhrātur dṛśyate puṇyakarmaṇaḥ
a yathā hīme vanasyāsya jñātāḥ pathi sahasraśaḥ
c saṃnatāḥ phalabhareṇa puṣpabhāreṇa ca drumāḥ
a pippalīnāṃ ca pakvānāṃ vanād asmād upāgataḥ
c gandho 'yaṃ pavanotkṣiptaḥ sahasā kaṭukodayaḥ
a tatra tatra ca dṛśyante saṃkṣiptāḥ kāṣṭhasaṃcayāḥ
c lūnāś ca pathi dṛśyante darbhā vaidūryavarcasaḥ
a etac ca vanamadhyasthaṃ kṛṣṇābhraśikharopamam
c pāvakasyāśramasthasya dhūmāgraṃ saṃpradṛśyate
a vivikteṣu ca tīrtheṣu kṛtasnānā dvijātayaḥ
c puṣpopahāraṃ kurvanti kusumaiḥ svayam ārjitaiḥ
a tat sutīkṣṇasya vacanaṃ yathā saumya mayā śrutam
c agastyasyāśramo bhrātur nūnam eṣa bhaviṣyati
a nigṛhya tarasā mṛtyuṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
c yasya bhrātrā kṛteyaṃ dik śaraṇyā puṇyakarmaṇā
a ihaikadā kila krūro vātāpir api celvalaḥ
c bhrātarau sahitāv āstāṃ brāhmaṇaghnau mahāsurau
a dhārayan brāhmaṇaṃ rūpam ilvalaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ vadan
c āmantrayati viprān sa śrāddham uddiśya nirghṛṇaḥ
a bhrātaraṃ saṃskṛtaṃ bhrātā tatas taṃ meṣarūpiṇam
c tān dvijān bhojayām āsa śrāddhadṛṣṭena karmaṇā
a tato bhuktavatāṃ teṣāṃ viprāṇām ilvalo 'bravīt
c vātāpe niṣkramasveti svareṇa mahatā vadan
a tato bhrātur vacaḥ śrutvā vātāpir meṣavan nadan
c bhittvā bhitvā śarīrāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ viniṣpatat
a brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasrāṇi tair evaṃ kāmarūpibhiḥ
c vināśitāni saṃhatya nityaśaḥ piśitāśanaiḥ
a agastyena tadā devaiḥ prārthitena maharṣiṇā
c anubhūya kila śrāddhe bhakṣitaḥ sa mahāsuraḥ
a tataḥ saṃpannam ity uktvā dattvā hastāvasecanam
c bhrātaraṃ niṣkramasveti ilvalaḥ so 'bhyabhāṣata
a taṃ tathā bhāṣamāṇaṃ tu bhrātaraṃ vipraghātinam
c abravīt prahasan dhīmān agastyo munisattamaḥ
a kuto niṣkramituṃ śaktir mayā jīrṇasya rakṣasaḥ
c bhrātus te meṣa rūpasya gatasya yamasādanam
a atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā bhrātur nidhanasaṃśritam
c pradharṣayitum ārebhe muniṃ krodhān niśācaraḥ
a so 'bhyadravad dvijendraṃ taṃ muninā dīptatejasā
c cakṣuṣānalakalpena nirdagdho nidhanaṃ gataḥ
a tasyāyam āśramo bhrātus taṭākavanaśobhitaḥ
c viprānukampayā yena karmedaṃ duṣkaraṃ kṛtam
a evaṃ kathayamānasya tasya saumitriṇā saha
c rāmasyāstaṃ gataḥ sūryaḥ saṃdhyākālo 'bhyavartata
a upāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ saha bhrātrā yathāvidhi
c praviveśāśramapadaṃ tam ṛṣiṃ cābhyavādayan
a samyak pratigṛhītas tu muninā tena rāghavaḥ
c nyavasat tāṃ niśām ekāṃ prāśya mūlaphalāni ca
a tasyāṃ rātryāṃ vyatītāyāṃ vimale sūryamaṇḍale
c bhrātaraṃ tam agastyasya āmantrayata rāghavaḥ
a abhivādaye tvā bhagavan sukham adhyuṣito niśām
c āmantraye tvāṃ gacchāmi guruṃ te draṣṭum agrajam
a gamyatām iti tenokto jagāma raghunandanaḥ
c yathoddiṣṭena mārgeṇa vanaṃ tac cāvalokayan
a nīvārān panasāṃs tālāṃs timiśān vañjulān dhavān
c ciribilvān madhūkāṃś ca bilvān api ca tindukān
a puṣpitān puṣpitāgrābhir latābhir anuveṣṭitān
c dadarśa rāmaḥ śataśas tatra kāntārapādapān
a hastihastair vimṛditān vānarair upaśobhitān
c mattaiḥ śakunisaṃghaiś ca śataśaḥ pratināditān
a tato 'bravīt samīpasthaṃ rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ
c pṛṣṭhato 'nugataṃ vīraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam
a snigdhapatrā yathā vṛkṣā yathā kṣāntā mṛgadvijāḥ
c āśramo nātidūrastho maharṣer bhāvitātmanaḥ
a agastya iti vikhyāto loke svenaiva karmaṇā
c āśramo dṛśyate tasya pariśrānta śramāpahaḥ
a prājyadhūmākulavanaś cīramālāpariṣkṛtaḥ
c praśāntamṛgayūthaś ca nānāśakunināditaḥ
a nigṛhya tarasā mṛtyuṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
c dakṣiṇā dik kṛtā yena śaraṇyā puṇyakarmaṇā
a tasyedam āśramapadaṃ prabhāvād yasya rākṣasaiḥ
c dig iyaṃ dakṣiṇā trāsād dṛśyate nopabhujyate
a yadā prabhṛti cākrāntā dig iyaṃ puṇyakarmaṇā
c tadā prabhṛti nirvairāḥ praśāntā rajanīcarāḥ
a nāmnā ceyaṃ bhagavato dakṣiṇā dik pradakṣiṇā
c prathitā triṣu lokeṣu durdharṣā krūrakarmabhiḥ
a mārgaṃ niroddhuṃ satataṃ bhāskarasyācalottamaḥ
c saṃdeśaṃ pālayaṃs tasya vindhyaśaulo na vardhate
a ayaṃ dīrghāyuṣas tasya loke viśrutakarmaṇaḥ
c agastyasyāśramaḥ śrīmān vinītamṛgasevitaḥ
a eṣa lokārcitaḥ sādhur hite nityaṃ rataḥ satām
c asmān adhigatān eṣa śreyasā yojayiṣyati
a ārādhayiṣyāmy atrāham agastyaṃ taṃ mahāmunim
c śeṣaṃ ca vanavāsasya saumya vatsyāmy ahaṃ prabho
a atra devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c agastyaṃ niyatāhāraṃ satataṃ paryupāsate
a nātra jīven mṛṣāvādī krūro vā yadi vā śaṭhaḥ
c nṛśaṃsaḥ kāma vṛtto vā munir eṣa tathāvidhaḥ
a atra devāś ca yakṣāś ca nāgāś ca patagaiḥ saha
c vasanti niyatāhāro dharmam ārādhayiṣṇavaḥ
a atra siddhā mahātmāno vimānaiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaiḥ
c tyaktvā dehān navair dehaiḥ svaryātāḥ paramarṣayaḥ
a yakṣatvam amaratvaṃ ca rājyāni vividhāni ca
c atra devāḥ prayacchanti bhūtair ārādhitāḥ śubhaiḥ
a āgatāḥ smāśramapadaṃ saumitre praviśāgrataḥ
c nivedayeha māṃ prāptam ṛṣaye saha sītayā
a sa praviśyāśramapadaṃ lakṣmaṇo rāghavānujaḥ
c agastyaśiṣyam āsādya vākyam etad uvāca ha
a rājā daśaratho nāma jyeṣṭhas tasya suto balī
c rāmaḥ prāpto muniṃ draṣṭuṃ bhāryayā saha sītayā
a lakṣmaṇo nāma tasyāhaṃ bhrātā tv avarajo hitaḥ
c anukūlaś ca bhaktaś ca yadi te śrotram āgataḥ
a te vayaṃ vanam atyugraṃ praviṣṭāḥ pitṛśāsanāt
c draṣṭum icchāmahe sarve bhagavantaṃ nivedyatām
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā lakṣmaṇasya tapodhanaḥ
c tathety uktvāgniśaraṇaṃ praviveśa niveditum
a sa praviśya muni śreṣṭhaṃ tapasā duṣpradharṣaṇam
c kṛtāñjalir uvācedaṃ rāmāgamanam añjasā
a putrau daśarathasyemau rāmo lakṣmaṇa eva ca
c praviṣṭāv āśramapadaṃ sītayā saha bhāryayā
a draṣṭuṃ bhavantam āyātau śuśrūṣārtham ariṃdamau
c yad atrānantaraṃ tattvam ājñāpayitum arhasi
a tataḥ śiṣyād upaśrutya prāptaṃ rāmaṃ salakṣmaṇam
c vaidehīṃ ca mahābhāgām idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a diṣṭyā rāmaś cirasyādya draṣṭuṃ māṃ samupāgataḥ
c manasā kāṅkṣitaṃ hy asya mayāpy āgamanaṃ prati
a gamyatāṃ satkṛto rāmaḥ sabhāryaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c praveśyatāṃ samīpaṃ me kiṃ cāsau na praveśitaḥ
a evam uktas tu muninā dharmajñena mahātmanā
c abhivādyābravīc chiṣyas tatheti niyatāñjaliḥ
a tato niṣkramya saṃbhrāntaḥ śiṣyo lakṣmaṇam abravīt
c kvāsau rāmo muniṃ draṣṭum etu praviśatu svayam
a tato gatvāśramapadaṃ śiṣyeṇa sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c darśayām āsa kākutsthaṃ sītāṃ ca janakātmajām
a taṃ śiṣyaḥ praśritaṃ vākyam agastyavacanaṃ bruvan
c prāveśayad yathānyāyaṃ satkārārthaṃ susatkṛtam
a praviveśa tato rāmaḥ sītayā sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c praśāntahariṇākīrṇam āśramaṃ hy avalokayan
a sa tatra brahmaṇaḥ sthānam agneḥ sthānaṃ tathaiva ca
c viṣṇoḥ sthānaṃ mahendrasya sthānaṃ caiva vivasvataḥ
a somasthānaṃ bhagasthānaṃ sthānaṃ kauberam eva ca
c dhātur vidhātuḥ sthānaṃ ca vāyoḥ sthānaṃ tathaiva ca
a tataḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto munir apy abhiniṣpatat
c taṃ dadarśāgrato rāmo munīnāṃ dīptatejasaṃ
e abravīd vacanaṃ vīro lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam
a eṣa lakṣmaṇa niṣkrāmaty agastyo bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c audāryeṇāvagacchāmi nidhānaṃ tapasām imam
a evam uktvā mahābāhur agastyaṃ sūryavarcasaṃ
c jagrāha paramaprītas tasya pādau paraṃtapaḥ
a abhivādya tu dharmātmā tasthau rāmaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
c sītayā saha vaidehyā tadā rāma salakṣmaṇaḥ
a pratigṛhya ca kākutstham arcayitvāsanodakaiḥ
c kuśalapraśnam uktvā ca āsyatām iti so 'bravīt
a agniṃ hutvā pradāyārghyam atithiṃ pratipūjya ca
c vānaprasthena dharmeṇa sa teṣāṃ bhojanaṃ dadau
a prathamaṃ copaviśyātha dharmajño munipuṃgavaḥ
c uvāca rāmam āsīnaṃ prāñjaliṃ dharmakovidam
a anyathā khalu kākutstha tapasvī samudācaran
c duḥsākṣīva pare loke svāni māṃsāni bhakṣayet
a rājā sarvasya lokasya dharmacārī mahārathaḥ
c pūjanīyaś ca mānyaś ca bhavān prāptaḥ priyātithiḥ
a evam uktvā phalair mūlaiḥ puṣpaiś cānyaiś ca rāghavam
c pūjayitvā yathākāmaṃ punar eva tato 'bravīt
a idaṃ divyaṃ mahac cāpaṃ hemavajravibhūṣitam
c vaiṣṇavaṃ puruṣavyāghra nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
a amoghaḥ sūryasaṃkāśo brahmadattaḥ śarottamaḥ
c datto mama mahendreṇa tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau
a saṃpūrṇau niśitair bāṇair jvaladbhir iva pāvakaiḥ
c mahārājata kośo 'yam asir hemavibhūṣitaḥ
a anena dhanuṣā rāma hatvā saṃkhye mahāsurān
c ājahāra śriyaṃ dīptāṃ purā viṣṇur divaukasām
a tad dhanus tau ca tūṇīrau śaraṃ khaḍgaṃ ca mānada
c jayāya pratigṛhṇīṣva vajraṃ vajradharo yathā
a evam uktvā mahātejāḥ samastaṃ tad varāyudham
c dattvā rāmāya bhagavān agastyaḥ punar abravīt
a rāma prīto 'smi bhadraṃ te parituṣṭo 'smi lakṣmaṇa
c abhivādayituṃ yan māṃ prāptau sthaḥ saha sītayā
a adhvaśrameṇa vāṃ khedo bādhate pracuraśramaḥ
c vyaktam utkaṇṭhate cāpi maithilī janakātmajā
a eṣā hi sukumārī ca duḥkhaiś ca na vimānitā
c prājyadoṣaṃ vanaṃ praptā bhartṛsnehapracoditā
a yathaiṣā ramate rāma iha sītā tathā kuru
c duṣkaraṃ kṛtavaty eṣā vane tvām anugacchatī
a eṣā hi prakṛtiḥ strīṇām āsṛṣṭe raghunandana
c samastham anurajyante viṣamasthaṃ tyajanti ca
a śatahradānāṃ lolatvaṃ śastrāṇāṃ tīkṣṇatāṃ tathā
c garuḍānilayoḥ śaighryam anugacchanti yoṣitaḥ
a iyaṃ tu bhavato bhāryā doṣair etair vivarjitāḥ
c ślāghyā ca vyapadeśyā ca yathā devī hy arundhatī
a alaṃkṛto 'yaṃ deśaś ca yatra saumitriṇā saha
c vaidehyā cānayā rāma vatsyasi tvam ariṃdama
a evam uktas tu muninā rāghavaḥ saṃyatāñjaliḥ
c uvāca praśritaṃ vākyam ṛṣiṃ dīptam ivānalam
a dhanyo 'smy anugṛhīto 'smi yasya me munipuṃgavaḥ
c guṇaiḥ sabhrātṛbhāryasya varadaḥ parituṣyati
a kiṃ tu vyādiśa me deśaṃ sodakaṃ bahukānanam
c yatrāśramapadaṃ kṛtvā vaseyaṃ nirataḥ sukham
a tato 'bravīn muni śreṣṭhaḥ śrutvā rāmasya bhāṣitam
c dhyātvā muhūrtaṃ dharmātmā dhīro dhīrataraṃ vacaḥ
a ito dviyojane tāta bahumūlaphalodakaḥ
c deśo bahumṛgaḥ śrīmān pañcavaṭy abhiviśrutaḥ
a tatra gatvāśramapadaṃ kṛtvā saumitriṇā saha
c ramasva tvaṃ pitur vākyaṃ yathoktam anupālayan
a vidito hy eṣa vṛttānto mama sarvas tavānagha
c tapasaś ca prabhāvena snehād daśarathasya ca
a hṛdayasthaś ca te chando vijñātas tapasā mayā
c iha vāsaṃ pratijñāya mayā saha tapovane
a ataś ca tvām ahaṃ brūmi gaccha pañcavaṭīm iti
c sa hi ramyo vanoddeśo maithilī tatra raṃsyate
a sa deśaḥ ślāghanīyaś ca nātidūre ca rāghava
c godāvaryāḥ samīpe ca maithilī tatra raṃsyate
a prājyamūlaphalaiś caiva nānādvija gaṇair yutaḥ
c viviktaś ca mahābāho puṇyo ramyas tathaiva ca
a bhavān api sadāraś ca śaktaś ca parirakṣaṇe
c api cātra vasan rāmas tāpasān pālayiṣyasi
a etad ālakṣyate vīra madhukānāṃ mahad vanam
c uttareṇāsya gantavyaṃ nyagrodham abhigacchatā
a tataḥ sthalam upāruhya parvatasyāvidūrataḥ
c khyātaḥ pañcavaṭīty eva nityapuṣpitakānanaḥ
a agastyenaivam uktas tu rāmaḥ saumitriṇā saha
c sātkṛtyāmantrayām āsa tam ṛṣiṃ satyavādinam
a tau tu tenābhyanujñātau kṛtapādābhivandanau
c tadāśramāt pañcavaṭīṃ jagmatuḥ saha sītayā
a gṛhītacāpau tu narādhipātmajau
viṣaktatūṇī samareṣv akātarau
c yathopadiṣṭena pathā maharṣiṇā
prajagmatuḥ pañcavaṭīṃ samāhitau
a atha pañcavaṭīṃ gacchann antarā raghunandanaḥ
c āsasāda mahākāyaṃ gṛdhraṃ bhīmaparākramam
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā tau mahābhāgau vanasthaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇau
c menāte rākṣasaṃ pakṣiṃ bruvāṇau ko bhavān iti
a sa tau madhurayā vācā saumyayā prīṇayann iva
c uvāca vatsa māṃ viddhi vayasyaṃ pitur ātmanaḥ
a sa taṃ pitṛsakhaṃ buddhvā pūjayām āsa rāghavaḥ
c sa tasya kulam avyagram atha papraccha nāma ca
a rāmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā kulam ātmānam eva ca
c ācacakṣe dvijas tasmai sarvabhūtasamudbhavam
a pūrvakāle mahābāho ye prajāpatayo 'bhavan
c tān me nigadataḥ sarvān āditaḥ śṛṇu rāghava
a kardamaḥ prathamas teṣāṃ vikṛtas tadanantaram
c śeṣaś ca saṃśrayaś caiva bahuputraś ca vīryavān
a sthāṇur marīcir atriś ca kratuś caiva mahābalaḥ
c pulastyaś cāṅgirāś caiva pracetāḥ pulahas tathā
a dakṣo vivasvān aparo 'riṣṭanemiś ca rāghava
c kaśyapaś ca mahātejās teṣām āsīc ca paścimaḥ
a prajāpates tu dakṣasya babhūvur iti naḥ śrutam
c ṣaṣṭir duhitaro rāma yaśasvinyo mahāyaśaḥ
a kaśyapaḥ pratijagrāha tāsām aṣṭau sumadhyamāḥ
c aditiṃ ca ditiṃ caiva danūm api ca kālakām
a tāmrāṃ krodhavaśāṃ caiva manuṃ cāpy analām api
c tās tu kanyās tataḥ prītaḥ kaśyapaḥ punar abravīt
a putrāṃs trailokyabhartṝn vai janayiṣyatha mat samān
c aditis tan manā rāma ditiś ca danur eva ca
a kālakā ca mahābāho śeṣās tv amanaso 'bhavan
c adityāṃ jajñire devās trayastriṃśad ariṃdama
a ādityā vasavo rudrā aśvinau ca paraṃtapa
c ditis tv ajanayat putrān daityāṃs tāta yaśasvinaḥ
a teṣām iyaṃ vasumatī purāsīt savanārṇavā
c danus tv ajanayat putram aśvagrīvam ariṃdama
a narakaṃ kālakaṃ caiva kālakāpi vyajāyata
c krauñcīṃ bhāsīṃ tathā śyenīṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrīṃ tathā śukīm
a tāmrāpi suṣuve kanyāḥ pañcaitā lokaviśrutāḥ
c ulūkāñ janayat krauñcī bhāsī bhāsān vyajāyata
a śyenī śyenāṃś ca gṛdhrāṃś ca vyajāyata sutejasaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭrī tu haṃsāṃś ca kalahaṃsāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
a cakravākāṃś ca bhadraṃ te vijajñe sāpi bhāminī
c śukī natāṃ vijajñe tu natāyā vinatā sutā
a daśakrodhavaśā rāma vijajñe 'py ātmasaṃbhavāḥ
c mṛgīṃ ca mṛgamandāṃ ca harīṃ bhadramadām api
a mātaṅgīm atha śārdūlīṃ śvetāṃ ca surabhīṃ tathā
c sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannāṃ surasāṃ kadrukām api
a apatyaṃ tu mṛgāḥ sarve mṛgyā naravarottama
c ṛṣkāś ca mṛgamandāyāḥ sṛmarāś camarās tathā
a tatas tv irāvatīṃ nāma jajñe bhadramadā sutām
c tasyās tv airāvataḥ putro lokanātho mahāgajaḥ
a haryāś ca harayo 'patyaṃ vānarāś ca tapasvinaḥ
c golāṅgūlāṃś ca śārdūlī vyāghrāṃś cājanayat sutān
a mātaṅgyās tv atha mātaṅgā apatyaṃ manujarṣabha
c diśāgajaṃ tu śvetākṣaṃ śvetā vyajanayat sutam
a tato duhitarau rāma surabhir devy ajāyata
c rohiṇīṃ nāma bhadraṃ te gandharvīṃ ca yaśasvinīm
a rohiṇy ajanayad gā vai gandharvī vājinaḥ sutān
c surasājanayan nāgān rāma kadrūś ca pannagān
a manur manuṣyāñ janayat kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ
c brāhmaṇān kṣatriyān vaiśyāñ śūdrāṃś ca manujarṣabha
a mukhato brāhmaṇā jātā urasaḥ kṣatriyās tathā
c ūrubhyāṃ jajñire vaiśyāḥ padbhyāṃ śūdrā iti śrutiḥ
a sarvān puṇyaphalān vṛkṣān analāpi vyajāyata
c vinatā ca śukī pautrī kadrūś ca surasā svasā
a kadrūr nāgasahaskraṃ tu vijajñe dharaṇīdharam
c dvau putrau vinatāyās tu garuḍo 'ruṇa eva ca
a tasmāj jāto 'ham aruṇāt saṃpātiś ca mamāgrajaḥ
c jaṭāyur iti māṃ viddhi śyenīputram ariṃdama
a so 'haṃ vāsasahāyas te bhaviṣyāmi yadīcchasi
c sītāṃ ca tāta rakṣiṣye tvayi yāte salakṣmaṇe
a jaṭāyuṣaṃ tu pratipūjya rāghavo
mudā pariṣvajya ca saṃnato 'bhavat
c pitur hi śuśrāva sakhitvam ātmavāñ
jaṭāyuṣā saṃkathitaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
a sa tatra sītāṃ paridāya maithilīṃ
sahaiva tenātibalena pakṣiṇā
c jagāma tāṃ pañcavaṭīṃ salakṣmaṇo
ripūn didhakṣañ śalabhān ivānalaḥ
a tataḥ pañcavaṭīṃ gatvā nānāvyālamṛgāyutām
c uvāca bhrātaraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasaṃ
a āgatāḥ sma yathoddiṣṭam amuṃ deśaṃ maharṣiṇā
c ayaṃ pañcavaṭī deśaḥ saumya puṣpitakānanaḥ
a sarvataś cāryatāṃ dṛṣṭiḥ kānane nipuṇo hy asi
c āśramaḥ katarasmin no deśe bhavati saṃmataḥ
a ramate yatra vaidehī tvam ahaṃ caiva lakṣmaṇa
c tādṛśo dṛśyatāṃ deśaḥ saṃnikṛṣṭajalāśayaḥ
a vanarāmaṇyakaṃ yatra jalarāmaṇyakaṃ tathā
c saṃnikṛṣṭaṃ ca yatra syāt samitpuṣpakuśodakam
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakmaṇaḥ saṃyatāñjaliḥ
c sītā samakṣaṃ kākutstham idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a paravān asmi kākutstha tvayi varṣaśataṃ sthite
c svayaṃ tu rucire deśe kriyatām iti māṃ vada
a suprītas tena vākyena lakṣmaṇasya mahādyutiḥ
c vimṛśan rocayām āsa deśaṃ sarvaguṇānvitam
a sa taṃ ruciram ākramya deśam āśramakarmaṇi
c haste gṛhītvā hastena rāmaḥ saumitrim abravīt
a ayaṃ deśaḥ samaḥ śrīmān puṣpitair tarubhir vṛtaḥ
c ihāśramapadaṃ saumya yathāvat kartum arhasi
a iyam ādityasaṃkāśaiḥ padmaiḥ surabhigandhibhiḥ
c adūre dṛśyate ramyā padminī padmaśobhitā
a yathākhyātam agastyena muninā bhāvitātmanā
c iyaṃ godāvarī ramyā puṣpitais tarubhir vṛtā
a haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇā cakravākopaśobhitā
c nātidūre na cāsanne mṛgayūthanipīḍitā
a mayūranāditā ramyāḥ prāṃśavo bahukandarāḥ
c dṛśyante girayaḥ saumya phullais tarubhir āvṛtāḥ
a sauvarṇe rājatais tāmrair deśe deśe ca dhātubhiḥ
c gavākṣitā ivābhānti gajāḥ paramabhaktibhiḥ
a sālais tālais tamālaiś ca kharjūraiḥ panasāmrakaiḥ
c nīvārais timiśaiś caiva puṃnāgaiś copaśobhitāḥ
a cūtair aśokais tilakaiś campakaiḥ ketakair api
c puṣpagulmalatopetais tais tais tarubhir āvṛtāḥ
a candanaiḥ syandanair nīpaiḥ panasair lakucair api
c dhavāśvakarṇakhadiraiḥ śamīkiṃśukapāṭalaiḥ
a idaṃ puṇyam idaṃ medhyam idaṃ bahumṛgadvijam
c iha vatsyāma saumitre sārdham etena pakṣiṇā
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahā
c acireṇāśramaṃ bhrātuś cakāra sumahābalaḥ
a parṇaśālāṃ suvipulāṃ tatra saṃghātamṛttikām
c sustambhāṃ maskarair dīrghaiḥ kṛtavaṃśāṃ suśobhanām
a sa gatvā lakṣmaṇaḥ śrīmān nadīṃ godāvarīṃ tadā
c snātvā padmāni cādāya saphalaḥ punar āgataḥ
a tataḥ puṣpabaliṃ kṛtvā śāntiṃ ca sa yathāvidhi
c darśayām āsa rāmāya tad āśramapadaṃ kṛtam
a sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtaṃ saumyam āśramaṃ saha sītayā
c rāghavaḥ parṇaśālāyāṃ harṣam āhārayat param
a susaṃhṛṣṭaḥ pariṣvajya bāhubhyāṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ tadā
c atisnigdhaṃ ca gāḍhaṃ ca vacanaṃ cedam abravīt
a prīto 'smi te mahat karma tvayā kṛtam idaṃ prabho
c pradeyo yannimittaṃ te pariṣvaṅgo mayā kṛtaḥ
a bhāvajñena kṛtajñena dharmajñena ca lakṣmaṇa
c tvayā putreṇa dharmātmā na saṃvṛttaḥ pitā mama
a evaṃ lakṣmaṇam uktvā tu rāghavo lakṣmivardhanaḥ
c tasmin deśe bahuphale nyavasat sa sukhaṃ vaśī
a kaṃ cit kālaṃ sa dharmātmā sītayā lakṣmaṇena ca
c anvāsyamāno nyavasat svargaloke yathāmaraḥ
a vasatas tasya tu mukhaṃ rāghavasya mahātmanaḥ
c śaradvyapāye hemanta ṛtur iṣṭaḥ pravartate
a sa kadā cit prabhātāyāṃ śarvaryāṃ raghunandanaḥ
c prayayāv abhiṣekārthaṃ ramyaṃ godāvarīṃ nadīm
a prahvaḥ kalaśahastas taṃ sītayā saha vīryavān
c pṛṣṭhato 'nuvrajan bhrātā saumitrir idam abravīt
a ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ priyo yas te priyaṃvada
c alaṃkṛta ivābhāti yena saṃvatsaraḥ śubhaḥ
a nīhāraparuṣo lokaḥ pṛṣhivī sasyamālinī
c jalāny anupabhogyāni subhago havyavāhanaḥ
a navāgrayaṇa pūjābhir abhyarcya pitṛdevatāḥ
c kṛtāgrayaṇakāḥ kāle santo vigatakalmaṣāḥ
a prājyakāmā janapadāḥ saṃpannataragorasāḥ
c vicaranti mahīpālā yātrārthaṃ vijigīṣavaḥ
a sevamāne dṛḍhaṃ sūrye diśam antakasevitām
c vihīnatilakeva strī nottarā dik prakāśate
a prakṛtyā himakośāḍhyo dūrasūryaś ca sāmpratam
c yathārthanāmā suvyaktaṃ himavān himavān giriḥ
a atyantasukhasaṃcārā madhyāhne sparśataḥ sukhāḥ
c divasāḥ subhagādityāś chāyāsaliladurbhagāḥ
a mṛdusūryāḥ sanīhārāḥ paṭuśītāḥ samārutāḥ
c śūnyāraṇyā himadhvastā divasā bhānti sāmpratam
a nivṛttākāśaśayanāḥ puṣyanītā himāruṇāḥ
c śītā vṛddhatarāyāmās triyāmā yānti sāmpratam
a ravisaṃkrāntasaubhābyas tuṣārāruṇamaṇḍalaḥ
c niḥśvāsāndha ivādarśaś candramā na prakāśate
a jyotsnā tuṣāramalinā paurṇamāsyāṃ na rājate
c sīteva cātapa śyāmā lakṣyate na tu śobhate
a prakṛtyā śītalasparśo himaviddhaś ca sāmpratam
c pravāti paścimo vāyuḥ kāle dviguṇaśītalaḥ
a bāṣpacchannān araṇyāni yavagodhūmavanti ca
c śobhante 'bhyudite sūrye nadadbhiḥ krauñcasārasaiḥ
a kharjūrapuṣpākṛtibhiḥ śirobhiḥ pūrṇataṇḍulaiḥ
c śobhante kiṃ cidālambāḥ śālayaḥ kanakaprabhāḥ
a mayūkhair upasarpadbhir himanīhārasaṃvṛtaiḥ
c dūram abhyuditaḥ sūryaḥ śaśāṅka iva lakṣyate
a agrāhyavīryaḥ pūrvāhṇe madhyāhne sparśataḥ sukhaḥ
c saṃraktaḥ kiṃ cid āpāṇḍur ātapaḥ śobhate kṣitau
a avaśyāyanipātena kiṃ cit praklinnaśādvalā
c vanānāṃ śobhate bhūmir niviṣṭataruṇātapā
a avaśyāyatamonaddhā nīhāratamasāvṛtāḥ
c prasuptā iva lakṣyante vipuṣpā vanarājayaḥ
a bāṣpasaṃchannasalilā rutavijñeyasārasāḥ
c himārdravālukais tīraiḥ sarito bhānti sāmpratam
a tuṣārapatanāc caiva mṛdutvād bhāskarasya ca
c śaityād agāgrastham api prāyeṇa rasavaj jalam
a jarājarjaritaiḥ parṇaiḥ śīrṇakesarakarṇikaiḥ
c nālaśeṣā himadhvastā na bhānti kamalākarāḥ
a asmiṃs tu puruṣavyāghra kāle duḥkhasamanvitaḥ
c tapaś carati dharmātmā tvadbhaktyā bharataḥ pure
a tyaktvā rājyaṃ ca mānaṃ ca bhogāṃś ca vividhān bahūn
c tapasvī niyatāhāraḥ śete śīte mahītale
a so 'pi velām imāṃ nūnam abhiṣekārtham udyataḥ
c vṛtaḥ prakṛtibhir nityaṃ prayāti sarayūṃ nadīm
a atyantasukhasaṃvṛddhaḥ sukumāro himārditaḥ
c kathaṃ tv apararātreṣu sarayūm avagāhate
a padmapatrekṣaṇaḥ śyāmaḥ śrīmān nirudaro mahān
c dharmajñaḥ satyavādī ca hrī niṣedho jitendriyaḥ
a priyābhibhāṣī madhuro dīrghabāhur ariṃdamaḥ
c saṃtyajya vividhān saukhyān āryaṃ sarvātmanāśritaḥ
a jitaḥ svargas tava bhrātrā bharatena mahātmanā
c vanastham api tāpasye yas tvām anuvidhīyate
a na pitryam anuvarntante mātṛkaṃ dvipadā iti
c khyāto lokapravādo 'yaṃ bharatenānyathākṛtaḥ
a bhartā daśaratho yasyāḥ sādhuś ca bharataḥ sutaḥ
c kathaṃ nu sāmbā kaikeyī tādṛśī krūradarśinī
a ity evaṃ lakṣmaṇe vākyaṃ snehād bruvati dharmike
c parivādaṃ jananyās tam asahan rāghavo 'bravīt
a na te 'mbā madhyamā tāta garhitavyā kathaṃ cana
c tām evekṣvākunāthasya bharatasya kathāṃ kuru
a niścitāpi hi me buddhir vanavāse dṛḍhavratā
c bharatasnehasaṃtaptā bāliśī kriyate punaḥ
a ity evaṃ vilapaṃs tatra prāpya godāvarīṃ nadīm
c cakre 'bhiṣekaṃ kākutsthaḥ sānujaḥ saha sītayā
a tarpayitvātha salilais te pitṝn daivatāni ca
c stuvanti smoditaṃ sūryaṃ devatāś ca samāhitāḥ
a kṛtābhiṣekaḥ sa rarāja rāmaḥ
sītādvitīyaḥ saha lakṣmaṇena
c kṛtābhiṣekas tv agarājaputryā
rudraḥ sanandir bhagavān iveśaḥ
a kṛtābhiṣeko rāmas tu sītā saumitrir eva ca
c tasmād godāvarītīrāt tato jagmuḥ svam āśramam
a āśramaṃ tam upāgamya rāghavaḥ sahalakṣmaṇaḥ
c kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ karma parṇaśālām upāgamat
a sa rāmaḥ parṇaśālāyām āsīnaḥ saha sītayā
c virarāja mahābāhuś citrayā candramā iva
e lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā cakāra vividhāḥ kathāḥ
a tadāsīnasya rāmasya kathāsaṃsaktacetasaḥ
c taṃ deśaṃ rākṣasī kā cid ājagāma yadṛcchayā
a sā tu śūrpaṇakhā nāma daśagrīvasya rakṣasaḥ
c bhaginī rāmam āsādya dadarśa tridaśopamam
a siṃhoraskaṃ mahābāhuṃ padmapatranibhekṣaṇam
c sukumāraṃ mahāsattvaṃ pārthivavyañjanānvitam
a rāmam indīvaraśyāmaṃ kandarpasadṛśaprabham
c babhūvendropamaṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasī kāmamohitā
a sumukhaṃ durmukhī rāmaṃ vṛttamadhyaṃ mahodarī
c viśālākṣaṃ virūpākṣī sukeśaṃ tāmramūrdhajā
a priyarūpaṃ virūpā sā susvaraṃ bhairavasnavā
c taruṇaṃ dāruṇā vṛddhā dakṣiṇaṃ vāmabhāṣiṇī
a nyāyavṛttaṃ sudurvṛttā priyam apriyadarśanā
c śarīrajasamāviṣṭā rākṣasī rāmam abravīt
a jaṭī tāpasarūpeṇa sabhāryaḥ śaracāpadhṛk
c āgatas tvam imaṃ deśaṃ kathaṃ rākṣasasevitam
a evam uktas tu rākṣasyā śūrpaṇakhyā paraṃtapaḥ
c ṛjubuddhitayā sarvam ākhyātum upacakrame
a āsīd daśaratho nāma rājā tridaśavikramaḥ
c tasyāham agrajaḥ putro rāmo nāma janaiḥ śrutaḥ
a bhrātāyaṃ lakṣmaṇo nāma yavīyān mām anuvrataḥ
c iyaṃ bhāryā ca vaidehī mama sīteti viśrutā
a niyogāt tu narendrasya pitur mātuś ca yantritaḥ
c dharmārthaṃ dharmakāṅkṣī ca vanaṃ vastum ihāgataḥ
a tvāṃ tu veditum icchāmi kathyatāṃ kāsi kasya vā
c iha vā kiṃnimittaṃ tvam āgatā brūhi tattvataḥ
a sābravīd vacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasī madanārditā
c śrūyatāṃ rāma vakṣyāmi tattvārthaṃ vacanaṃ mama
a ahaṃ śūrpaṇakhā nāma rākṣasī kāmarūpiṇī
c araṇyaṃ vicarāmīdam ekā sarvabhayaṃkarā
a rāvaṇo nāma me bhrātā rākṣaso rākṣaseśvaraḥ
c pravṛddhanidraś ca sadā kumbhakarṇo mahābalaḥ
a vibhīṣaṇas tu dharmātmā na tu rākṣasaceṣṭitaḥ
c prakhyātavīryau ca raṇe bhrātarau kharadūṣaṇau
a tān ahaṃ samatikrāntā rāma tvāpūrvadarśanāt
c samupetāsmi bhāvena bhartāraṃ puruṣottamam
e cirāya bhava bhartā me sītayā kiṃ kariṣyasi
a vikṛtā ca virūpā ca na seyaṃ sadṛśī tava
c aham evānurūpā te bhāryā rūpeṇa paśya mām
a imāṃ virūpām asatīṃ karālāṃ nirṇatodarīm
c anena saha te bhrātrā bhakṣayiṣyāmi mānuṣīm
a tataḥ parvataśṛṅgāṇi vanāni vividhāni ca
c paśyan saha mayā kānta daṇḍakān vicariṣyasi
a ity evam uktaḥ kākutsthaḥ prahasya madirekṣaṇām
c idaṃ vacanam ārebhe vaktuṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
a tāṃ tu śūrpaṇakhāṃ rāmaḥ kāmapāśāvapāśitām
c svecchayā ślakṣṇayā vācā smitapūrvam athābravīt
a kṛtadāro 'smi bhavati bhāryeyaṃ dayitā mama
c tvadvidhānāṃ tu nārīṇāṃ suduḥkhā sasapatnatā
a anujas tv eṣa me bhrātā śīlavān priyadarśanaḥ
c śrīmān akṛtadāraś ca lakṣmaṇo nāma vīryavān
a apūrvī bhāryayā cārthī taruṇaḥ priyadarśanaḥ
c anurūpaś ca te bhartā rūpasyāsya bhaviṣyati
a enaṃ bhaja viśālākṣi bhartāraṃ bhrātaraṃ mama
c asapatnā varārohe merum arkaprabhā yathā
a iti rāmeṇa sā proktā rākṣasī kāmamohitā
c visṛjya rāmaṃ sahasā tato lakṣmaṇam abravīt
a asya rūpasya te yuktā bhāryāhaṃ varavarṇinī
c mayā saha sukhaṃ sarvān daṇḍakān vicariṣyasi
a evam uktas tu saumitrī rākṣasyā vākyakovidaḥ
c tataḥ śūrpaṇakhīṃ smitvā lakṣmaṇo yuktam abravīt
a kathaṃ dāsasya me dāsī bhāryā bhavitum icchasi
c so 'ham āryeṇa paravān bhātrā kamalavarṇinī
a samṛddhārthasya siddhārthā muditāmalavarṇinī
c āryasya tvaṃ viśālākṣi bhāryā bhava yavīyasī
a etāṃ virūpām asatīṃ karālāṃ nirṇatodarīm
c bhāryāṃ vṛddhāṃ parityajya tvām evaiṣa bhajiṣyati
a ko hi rūpam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ saṃtyajya varavarṇini
c mānuṣeṣu varārohe kuryād bhāvaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ
a iti sā lakṣmaṇenoktā karālā nirṇatodarī
c manyate tad vacaḥ satyaṃ parihāsāvicakṣaṇā
a sā rāmaṃ parṇaśālāyām upaviṣṭaṃ paraṃtapam
c sītayā saha durdharṣam abravīt kāmamohitā
a imāṃ virūpām asatīṃ karālāṃ nirṇatodarīm
c vṛddhāṃ bhāryām avaṣṭabhya na māṃ tvaṃ bahu manyase
a adyemāṃ bhakṣayiṣyāmi paśyatas tava mānuṣīm
c tvayā saha cariṣyāmi niḥsapatnā yathāsukham
a ity uktvā mṛgaśāvākṣīm alātasadṛśekṣaṇā
c abhyadhāvat susaṃkruddhā maholkā rohiṇīm iva
a tāṃ mṛtyupāśapratimām āpatantīṃ mahābalaḥ
c nigṛhya rāmaḥ kupitas tato lakṣmaṇam abravīt
a krūrair anāryaiḥ saumitre parihāsaḥ kathaṃ cana
c na kāryaḥ paśya vaidehīṃ kathaṃ cit saumya jīvatīm
a imāṃ virūpām asatīm atimattāṃ mahodarīm
c rākṣasīṃ puruṣavyāghra virūpayitum arhasi
a ity ukto lakṣmaṇas tasyāḥ kruddho rāmasya paśyataḥ
c uddhṛtya khaḍgaṃ ciccheda karṇanāsaṃ mahābalaḥ
a nikṛttakarṇanāsā tu visvaraṃ sā vinadya ca
c yathāgataṃ pradudrāva ghorā śūrpaṇakhā vanam
a sā virūpā mahāghorā rākṣasī śoṇitokṣitā
c nanāda vividhān nādān yathā prāvṛṣi toyadaḥ
a sā vikṣarantī rudhiraṃ bahudhā ghoradarśanā
c pragṛhya bāhū garjantī praviveśa mahāvanam
a tatas tu sā rākṣasasaṃgha saṃvṛtaṃ
kharaṃ janasthānagataṃ virūpitā
c upetya taṃ bhrātaram ugratejasaṃ
papāta bhūmau gaganād yathāśaniḥ
a tataḥ sabhāryaṃ bhayamohamūrchitā
salakṣmaṇaṃ rāghavam āgataṃ vanam
c virūpaṇaṃ cātmani śoṇitokṣitā
śaśaṃsa sarvaṃ bhaginī kharasya sā
a tāṃ tathā patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā virūpāṃ śoṇitokṣitām
c bhaginīṃ krodhasaṃtaptaḥ kharaḥ papraccha rākṣasaḥ
a balavikramasaṃpannā kāmagā kāmarūpiṇī
c imām avasthāṃ nītā tvaṃ kenāntakasamā gatā
a devagandharvabhūtānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanām
c ko 'yam evaṃ mahāvīryas tvāṃ virūpāṃ cakāra ha
a na hi paśyāmy ahaṃ loke yaḥ kuryān mama vipriyam
c antarena sahasrākṣaṃ mahendraṃ pākaśāsanam
a adyāhaṃ mārgaṇaiḥ prāṇān ādāsye jīvitāntakaiḥ
c salile kṣīram āsaktaṃ niṣpibann iva sārasaḥ
a nihatasya mayā saṃkhye śarasaṃkṛttamarmaṇaḥ
c saphenaṃ rudhiraṃ raktaṃ medinī kasya pāsyati
a kasya patrarathāḥ kāyān māṃsam utkṛtya saṃgatāḥ
c prahṛṣṭā bhakṣayiṣyanti nihatasya mayā raṇe
a taṃ na devā na gandharvā na piśācā na rākṣasāḥ
c mayāpakṛṣṭaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ śaktās trātuṃ mahāhave
a upalabhya śanaiḥ saṃjñāṃ taṃ me śaṃsitum arhasi
c yena tvaṃ durvinītena vane vikramya nirjitā
a iti bhrātur vacaḥ śrutvā kruddhasya ca viśeṣataḥ
c tataḥ śūrpaṇakhā vākyaṃ sabāṣpam idam abravīt
a taruṇau rūpasaṃpannau sukūmārau mahābalau
c puṇḍarīkaviśālākṣau cīrakṛṣṇājināmbarau
a gandharvarājapratimau pārthivavyañjanānvitau
c devau vā mānuṣau vā tau na tarkayitum utsahe
a taruṇī rūpasaṃpannā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitā
c dṛṣṭā tatra mayā nārī tayor madhye sumadhyamā
a tābhyām ubhābhyāṃ saṃbhūya pramadām adhikṛtya tām
c imām avasthāṃ nītāhaṃ yathānāthāsatī tathā
a tasyāś cānṛjuvṛttāyās tayoś ca hatayor aham
c saphenaṃ pātum icchāmi rudhiraṃ raṇamūrdhani
a eṣa me prathamaḥ kāmaḥ kṛtas tāta tvayā bhavet
c tasyās tayoś ca rudhiraṃ pibeyam aham āhave
a iti tasyāṃ bruvāṇāyāṃ caturdaśa mahābalān
c vyādideśa kharaḥ kruddho rākṣasān antakopamān
a mānuṣau śastrasaṃpannau cīrakṛṣṇājināmbarau
c praviṣṭau daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ ghoraṃ pramadayā saha
a tau hatvā tāṃ ca durvṛttām upāvartitum arhatha
c iyaṃ ca rudhiraṃ teṣāṃ bhaginī mama pāsyati
a manoratho 'yam iṣṭo 'syā bhaginyā mama rākṣasāḥ
c śīghraṃ saṃpadyatāṃ gatvā tau pramathya svatejasā
a iti pratisamādiṣṭā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
c tatra jagmus tayā sārdhaṃ ghanā vāteritā yathā
a tataḥ śūrpaṇakhā ghorā rāghavāśramam āgatā
c rakṣasām ācacakṣe tau bhrātarau saha sītayā
a te rāmaṃ parṇaśālāyām upaviṣṭaṃ mahābalam
c dadṛśuḥ sītayā sārdhaṃ vaidehyā lakṣmaṇena ca
a tān dṛṣṭvā rāghavaḥ śrīmān āgatāṃ tāṃ ca rākṣasīm
c abravīd bhrātaraṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ dīptatejasaṃ
a muhūrtaṃ bhava saumitre sītāyāḥ pratyanantaraḥ
c imān asyā vadhiṣyāmi padavīm āgatān iha
a vākyam etat tataḥ śrutvā rāmasya viditātmanaḥ
c tatheti lakṣmaṇo vākyaṃ rāmasya pratyapūjayat
a rāghavo 'pi mahac cāpaṃ cāmīkaravibhūṣitam
c cakāra sajyaṃ dharmātmā tāni rakṣāṃsi cābravīt
a putrau daśarathasyāvāṃ bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇau
c praviṣṭau sītayā sārdhaṃ duścaraṃ daṇḍakāvanam
a phalamūlāśanau dāntau tāpasau dharmacāriṇau
c vasantau daṇḍakāraṇye kimartham upahiṃsatha
a yuṣmān pāpātmakān hantuṃ viprakārān mahāvane
c ṛṣīṇāṃ tu niyogena prāpto 'haṃ saśarāsanaḥ
a tiṣṭhataivātra saṃtuṣṭā nopasarpitum arhatha
c yadi prāṇair ihārtho vo nivartadhvaṃ niśācarāḥ
a tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
c ūcur vācaṃ susaṃkruddhā brahmaghnaḥ śūlapāṇayaḥ
a saṃraktanayanā ghorā rāmaṃ raktāntalocanam
c paruṣā madhurābhāṣaṃ hṛṣṭādṛṣṭaparākramam
a krodham utpādya no bhartuḥ kharasya sumahātmanaḥ
c tvam eva hāsyase prāṇān adyāsmābhir hato yudhi
a kā hi te śaktir ekasya bahūnāṃ raṇamūrdhani
c asmākam agrataḥ sthātuṃ kiṃ punar yoddhum āhave
a ebhir bāhuprayuktair naḥ parighaiḥ śūlapaṭṭiśaiḥ
c prāṇāṃs tyakṣyasi vīryaṃ ca dhanuś ca karapīḍitam
a ity evam uktvā saṃrabdhā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
c udyatāyudhanistriṃśā rāmam evābhidudruvuḥ
e cikṣipus tāni śūlāni rāghavaṃ prati durjayam
a tāni śūlāni kākutsthaḥ samastāni caturdaśa
c tāvadbhir eva ciccheda śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥ
a tataḥ paścān mahātejā nārācān sūryasaṃnibhān
c jagrāha paramakruddhaś caturdaśa śilāśitān
a gṛhītvā dhanur āyamya lakṣyān uddiśya rākṣasān
c mumoca rāghavo bāṇān vajrān iva śatakratuḥ
a rukmapuṅkhāś ca viśikhāḥ pradīptā hemabhūṣaṇāḥ
c antarikṣe maholkānāṃ babhūvus tulyavarcasaḥ
a te bhittvā rakṣasāṃ vegād vakṣāṃsi rudhirāplutāḥ
c viniṣpetus tadā bhūmau nyamajjantāśanisvanāḥ
a te bhinnahṛdayā bhūmau chinnamūlā iva drumāḥ
c nipetuḥ śoṇitārdrāṅgā vikṛtā vigatāsavaḥ
a tān bhūmau patitān dṛṣṭvā rākṣasī krodhamūrchitā
c paritrastā punas tatra vyasṛjad bhairavaṃ ravam
a sā nadantī mahānādaṃ javāc chūrpaṇakhā punaḥ
c upagamya kharaṃ sā tu kiṃ cit saṃśuṣka śoṇitā
e papāta punar evārtā saniryāseva vallarī
a nipātitān prekṣya raṇe tu rākṣasān
pradhāvitā śūrpaṇakhā punas tataḥ
c vadhaṃ ca teṣāṃ nikhilena rakṣasāṃ
śaśaṃsa sarvaṃ bhaginī kharasya sā
a sa punaḥ patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā krodhāc chūrpaṇakhāṃ kharaḥ
c uvāca vyaktatā vācā tām anarthārtham āgatām
a mayā tv idānīṃ śūrās te rākṣasā rudhirāśanāḥ
c tvatpriyārthaṃ vinirdiṣṭāḥ kimarthaṃ rudyate punaḥ
a bhaktāś caivānuraktāś ca hitāś ca mama nityaśaḥ
c ghnanto 'pi na nihantavyā na na kuryur vaco mama
a kim etac chrotum icchāmi kāraṇaṃ yatkṛte punaḥ
c hā nātheti vinardantī sarpavad veṣṭase kṣitau
a anāthavad vilapasi kiṃ nu nāthe mayi sthite
c uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha mā bhaiṣīr vaiklavyaṃ tyajyatām iha
a ity evam uktā durdharṣā khareṇa parisāntvitā
c vimṛjya nayane sāsre kharaṃ bhrātaram abravīt
a preṣitāś ca tvayā śūrā rākṣasās te caturdaśa
c nihantuṃ rāghavaṃ ghorā matpriyārthaṃ salakṣmaṇam
a te tu rāmeṇa sāmarṣāḥ śūlapaṭṭiśapāṇayaḥ
c samare nihatāḥ sarve sāyakair marmabhedibhiḥ
a tān bhūmau patitān dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇenaiva mahābalān
c rāmasya ca mahat karma mahāṃs trāso 'bhavan mama
a sāsmi bhītā samudvignā viṣaṇṇā ca niśācara
c śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ punaḥ prāptā sarvato bhayadarśinī
a viṣādanakrādhyuṣite paritrāsormimālini
c kiṃ māṃ na trāyase magnāṃ vipule śokasāgare
a ete ca nihatā bhūmau rāmeṇa niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
c ye ca me padavīṃ prāptā rākṣasāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
a mayi te yady anukrośo yadi rakṣaḥsu teṣu ca
c rāmeṇa yadi śaktis te tejo vāsti niśācara
e daṇḍakāraṇyanilayaṃ jahi rākṣasakaṇṭakam
a yadi rāmaṃ mamāmitram adya tvaṃ na vadhiṣyasi
c tava caivāgrataḥ prāṇāṃs tyakṣyāmi nirapatrapā
a buddhyāham anupaśyāmi na tvaṃ rāmasya saṃyuge
c sthātuṃ pratimukhe śaktaḥ sacāpasya mahāraṇe
a śūramānī na śūras tvaṃ mithyāropitavikramaḥ
c mānuṣau yan na śaknoṣi hantuṃ tau rāmalakṣmaṇau
a apayāhi janasthānāt tvaritaḥ sahabāndhavaḥ
c niḥsattvasyālpavīryasya vāsas te kīdṛśas tv iha
a rāmatejo'bhibhūto hi tvaṃ kṣipraṃ vinaśiṣyasi
c sa hi tejaḥsamāyukto rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ
e bhrātā cāsya mahāvīryo yena cāsmi virūpitā
a evam ādharṣitaḥ śūraḥ śūrpaṇakhyā kharas tadā
c uvāca rakṣasāṃ madhye kharaḥ kharataraṃ vacaḥ
a tavāpamānaprabhavaḥ krodho 'yam atulo mama
c na śakyate dhārayituṃ lavaṇāmbha ivotthitam
a na rāmaṃ gaṇaye vīryān mānuṣaṃ kṣīṇajīvitam
c ātmā duścaritaiḥ prāṇān hato yo 'dya vimokṣyati
a bāṣpaḥ saṃhriyatām eṣa saṃbhramaś ca vimucyatām
c ahaṃ rāmaḥ saha bhrātrā nayāmi yamasādanam
a paraśvadhahatasyādya mandaprāṇasya bhūtale
c rāmasya rudhiraṃ raktam uṣṇaṃ pāsyasi rākṣasi
a sā prahṛṣṭvā vacaḥ śrutvā kharasya vadanāc cyutam
c praśaśaṃsa punar maurkhyād bhrātaraṃ rakṣasāṃ varam
a tayā paruṣitaḥ pūrvaṃ punar eva praśaṃsitaḥ
c abravīd dūṣaṇaṃ nāma kharaḥ senāpatiṃ tadā
a caturdaśa sahasrāṇi mama cittānuvartinām
c rakṣasīṃ bhīmavegānāṃ samareṣv anivartinām
a nīlajīmūtavarṇānāṃ ghorāṇāṃ krūrakarmaṇām
c lokasiṃhāvihārāṇāṃ balinām ugratejasām
a teṣāṃ śārdūladarpāṇāṃ mahāsyānāaṃ mahaujasām
c sarvodyogam udīrṇānāṃ rakṣasāṃ saumya kāraya
a upasthāpaya me kṣipraṃ rathaṃ saumya dhanūṃṣi ca
c śarāṃś ca citrān khaḍgāṃś ca śaktīś ca vividhāḥ śitāḥ
a agre niryātum icchāmi paulastyānāṃ mahātmanām
c vadhārthaṃ durvinītasya rāmasya raṇakovidaḥ
a iti tasya bruvāṇasya sūryavarṇaṃ mahāratham
c sadaśvaiḥ śabalair yuktam ācacakṣe 'tha dūṣaṇaḥ
a taṃ meruśikharākāraṃ taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇam
c hemacakram asaṃbādhaṃ vaidūryamaya kūbaram
a matsyaiḥ puṣpair drumaiḥ śailaiś candrasūryaiś ca kāñcanaiḥ
c māṅgalyaiḥ pakṣisaṃghaiś ca tārābhiś ca samāvṛtam
a dhvajanistriṃśasaṃpannaṃ kiṅkiṇīkavibhūṣitam
c sadaśvayuktaṃ so 'marṣād āruroha rathaṃ kharaḥ
a niśāmya taṃ rathagataṃ rāakṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ
c tasthuḥ saṃparivāryainaṃ dūṣaṇaṃ ca mahābalam
a kharas tu tān maheṣvāsān ghoracarmāyudhadhvajān
c niryātety abravīd dṛṣṭvā rathasthaḥ sarvarākṣasān
a tatas tad rākṣasaṃ sainyaṃ ghoracarmāyudhadhvajam
c nirjagāma janasthānān mahānādaṃ mahājavam
a mudgaraiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ śūlaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
c khaḍgaiś cakraiś ca hastasthair bhrājamānaiś ca tomaraiḥ
a śaktibhiḥ patighair ghorair atimātraiś ca kārmukaiḥ
c gadāsimusalair vajrair gṛhītair bhīmadarśanaiḥ
a rākṣasānāṃ sughorāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa
c niryātāni janasthānāt kharacittānuvartinām
a tāṃs tv abhidravato dṛṣṭvā rākṣasān bhīmavikramān
c kharasyāpi rathaḥ kiṃ cij jagāma tadanantaram
a tatas tāñ śabalān aśvāṃs taptakāñcanabhūṣitān
c kharasya matam ājñāya sārathiḥ samacodayat
a sa codito rathaḥ śīghraṃ kharasya ripughātinaḥ
c śabdenāpūrayām āsa diśaś ca pratiśas tathā
a pravṛddhamanyus tu kharaḥ kharasvano
ripor vadhārthaṃ tvarito yathāntakaḥ
c acūcudat sārathim unnadan punar
mahābalo megha ivāśmavarṣavān
a tat prayātaṃ balaṃ ghoram aśivaṃ śoṇitodakam
c abhyavarṣan mahāmeghas tumulo gardabhāruṇaḥ
a nipetus turagās tasya rathayuktā mahājavāḥ
c same puṣpacite deśe rājamārge yadṛcchayā
a śyāmaṃ rudhiraparyantaṃ babhūva pariveṣaṇam
c alātacakrapratimaṃ pratigṛhya divākaram
a tato dhvajam upāgamya hemadaṇḍaṃ samucchritam
c samākramya mahākāyas tasthau gṛdhraḥ sudāruṇaḥ
a janasthānasamīpe ca samākramya kharasvanāḥ
c visvarān vividhāṃś cakrur māṃsādā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
a vyājahruś ca padīptāyāṃ diśi vai bhairavasvanam
c aśivā yātu dāhānāṃ śivā ghorā mahāsvanāḥ
a prabhinnagirisaṃkāśās toyaśoṣitadhāriṇaḥ
c ākāśaṃ tad anākāśaṃ cakrur bhīmā balāhakāḥ
a babhūva timiraṃ ghoram uddhataṃ romaharṣaṇam
c diśo vā vidiśo vāpi suvyaktaṃ na cakāśire
a kṣatajārdrasavarṇābhā saṃdhyākālaṃ vinā babhau
c kharasyābhimukhaṃ nedus tadā ghorā mṛgāḥ khagāḥ
a nityāśivakarā yuddhe śivā ghoranidarśanāḥ
c nedur balasyābhimukhaṃ jvālodgāribhir ānanaiḥ
a kabandhaḥ parighābhāso dṛśyate bhāskarāntike
c jagrāha sūryaṃ svarbhānur aparvaṇi mahāgrahaḥ
a pravāti mārutaḥ śīghraṃ niṣprabho 'bhūd divākaraḥ
c utpetuś ca vinā rātriṃ tārāḥ khadyotasaprabhāḥ
a saṃlīnamīnavihagā nalinyaḥ puṣpapaṅkajāḥ
c tasmin kṣaṇe babhūvuś ca vinā puṣpaphalair drumāḥ
a uddhūtaś ca vinā vātaṃ reṇur jaladharāruṇaḥ
c vīcīkūcīti vāśyanto babhūvus tatra sārikāḥ
a ulkāś cāpi sanirghoṣā nipetur ghoradarśanāḥ
c pracacāla mahī cāpi saśailavanakānanā
a kharasya ca rathasthasya nardamānasya dhīmataḥ
c prākampata bhujaḥ savyaḥ kharaś cāsyāvasajjata
a sāsrā saṃpadyate dṛṣṭiḥ paśyamānasya sarvataḥ
c lalāṭe ca rujā jātā na ca mohān nyavartata
a tān samīkṣya mahotpātān utthitān romaharṣaṇān
c abravīd rākṣasān sarvān prahasan sa kharas tadā
a mahotpātān imān sarvān utthitān ghoradarśanān
c na cintayāmy ahaṃ vīryād balavān durbalān iva
a tārā api śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ pātayeyaṃ nabhastalāt
c mṛtyuṃ maraṇadharmeṇa saṃkruddho yojayāmy aham
a rāghavaṃ taṃ balotsiktaṃ bhrātaraṃ cāpi lakṣmaṇam
c ahatvā sāyakais tīkṣṇair nopāvartitum utsahe
a sakāmā bhaginī me 'stu pītvā tu rudhiraṃ tayoḥ
c yannimittaṃ tu rāmasya lakṣmaṇasya viparyayaḥ
a na kva cit prāptapūrvo me saṃyugeṣu parājayaḥ
c yuṣmākam etat pratyakṣaṃ nānṛtaṃ kathayāmy aham
a devarājam api kruddho mattairāvatayāyinam
c vajrahastaṃ raṇe hanyāṃ kiṃ punas tau ca mānuṣau
a sā tasya garjitaṃ śrutvā rākṣasasya mahācamūḥ
c praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe mṛtyupāśāvapāśitā
a sameyuś ca mahātmāno yuddhadarśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
c ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥ
a sametya coruḥ sahitās te 'nyāyaṃ puṇyakarmaṇaḥ
c svasti gobrāhmaṇebhyo 'stu lokānāṃ ye ca saṃmatāḥ
a jayatāṃ rāghavo yuddhe paulastyān rajanīcarān
c cakrā hasto yathā yuddhe sarvān asurapuṃgavān
a etac cānyac ca bahuśo bruvāṇāḥ paramarṣayaḥ
c dadṛśur vāhinīṃ teṣāṃ rākṣasānāṃ gatāyuṣām
a rathena tu kharo vegāt sainyasyāgrād viniḥsṛtaḥ
c taṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ bhūyo rākṣasāś ca viniḥsṛtāḥ
a śyena gāmī pṛthugrīvo yajñaśatrur vihaṃgamaḥ
c durjayaḥ karavīrākṣaḥ paruṣaḥ kālakārmukaḥ
a meghamālī mahāmālī sarpāsyo rudhirāśanaḥ
c dvādaśaite mahāvīryāḥ pratasthur abhitaḥ kharam
a mahākapālaḥ sthūlākṣaḥ pramāthī triśirās tathā
c catvāra ete senāgryā dūṣaṇaṃ pṛṣṭhato 'nvayuḥ
a sā bhīmavegā samarābhikāmā
sudāruṇā rākṣasavīra senā
c tau rājaputrau sahasābhyupetā
mālāgrahāṇām iva candrasūryau
a āśramaṃ prati yāte tu khare kharaparākrame
c tān evautpātikān rāmaḥ saha bhrātrā dadarśa ha
a tān utpātān mahāghorān utthitān romaharṣaṇān
c prajānām ahitān dṛṣṭvā vākyaṃ lakṣmaṇam abravīt
a imān paśya mahābāho sarvabhūtāpahāriṇaḥ
c samutthitān mahotpātān saṃhartuṃ sarvarākṣasān
a amī rudhiradhārās tu visṛjantaḥ kharasvanān
c vyomni meghā vivartante paruṣā gardabhāruṇāḥ
a sadhūmāś ca śarāḥ sarve mama yuddhābhinandinaḥ
c rukmapṛṣṭhāni cāpāni viveṣṭante ca lakṣmaṇa
a yādṛśā iha kūjanti pakṣiṇo vanacāriṇaḥ
c agrato no bhayaṃ prāptaṃ saṃśayo jīvitasya ca
a saṃprahāras tu sumahān bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
c ayam ākhyāti me bāhuḥ sphuramāṇo muhur muhuḥ
a saṃnikarṣe tu naḥ śūra jayaṃ śatroḥ parājayam
c suprabhaṃ ca prasannaṃ ca tava vaktraṃ hi lakṣyate
a udyatānāṃ hi yuddhārthaṃ yeṣāṃ bhavati lakṣmaṇaḥ
c niṣprabhaṃ vadanaṃ teṣāṃ bhavaty āyuḥ parikṣayaḥ
a anāgatavidhānaṃ tu kartavyaṃ śubham icchatā
c āpadaṃ śaṅkamānena puruṣeṇa vipaścitā
a tasmād gṛhītvā vaidehīṃ śarapāṇir dhanurdharaḥ
c guhām āśrayaśailasya durgāṃ pādapasaṃkulām
a pratikūlitum icchāmi na hi vākyam idaṃ tvayā
c śāpito mama pādābhyāṃ gamyatāṃ vatsa māciram
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa lakṣmaṇaḥ saha sītayā
c śarān ādāya cāpaṃ ca guhāṃ durgāṃ samāśrayat
a tasmin praviṣṭe tu guhāṃ lakṣmaṇe saha sītayā
c hanta niryuktam ity uktvā rāmaḥ kavacam āviśat
a sā tenāgninikāśena kavacena vibhūṣitaḥ
c babhūva rāmas timire vidhūmo 'gnir ivotthitaḥ
a sa cāpam udyamya mahac charān ādāya vīryavān
c babhūvāvasthitas tatra jyāsvanaiḥ pūrayan diśaḥ
a tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca saha cāraṇaiḥ
c ūcuḥ paramasaṃtrastā guhyakāś ca parasparam
a caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
c ekaś ca rāmo dharmātmā kathaṃ yuddhaṃ bhaviṣyati
a tato gambhīranirhrādaṃ ghoravarmāyudhadhvajam
c anīkaṃ yātudhānānāṃ samantāt pratyadṛśyata
a siṃhanādaṃ visṛjatām anyonyam abhigarjatām
c cāpāni vispharayatāṃ jṛmbhatāṃ cāpy abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
a vipraghuṣṭasvanānāṃ ca dundubhīṃś cāpi nighnatām
c teṣāṃ sutumulaḥ śabdaḥ pūrayām āsa tad vanam
a tena śabdena vitrastāḥ śvāpadā vanacāriṇaḥ
c dudruvur yatra niḥśabdaṃ pṛṣṭhato nāvalokayan
a tat tv anīkaṃ mahāvegaṃ rāmaṃ samupasarpata
c ghṛtanānāpraharaṇaṃ gambhīraṃ sāgaropamam
a rāmo 'pi cārayaṃś cakṣuḥ sarvato raṇapaṇḍitaḥ
c dadarśa kharasainyaṃ tad yuddhābhimukham udyatam
a vitatya ca dhanur bhīmaṃ tūṇyāś coddhṛtya sāyakān
c krodham āhārayat tīvraṃ vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām
a duṣprekṣyaḥ so 'bhavat kruddho yugāntāgnir iva jvalan
c taṃ dṛṣṭvā tejasāviṣṭaṃ prāvyathan vanadevatāḥ
a tasya kruddhasya rūpaṃ tu rāmasya dadṛśe tadā
c dakṣasyeva kratuṃ hantum udyatasya pinākinaḥ
a avaṣṭabdhadhanuṃ rāmaṃ kruddhaṃ ca ripughātinam
c dadarśāśramam āgamya kharaḥ saha puraḥsaraiḥ
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā saguṇaṃ cāpam udyamya kharaniḥsvanam
c rāmasyābhimukhaṃ sūtaṃ codyatām ity acodayat
a sa kharasyājñayā sūtas turagān samacodayat
c yatra rāmo mahābāhur eko dhunvan dhanuḥ sthitaḥ
a taṃ tu niṣpatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te rajanīcarāḥ
c nardamānā mahānādaṃ sacivāḥ paryavārayan
a sa teṣāṃ yātudhānānāṃ madhye rato gataḥ kharaḥ
c babhūva madhye tārāṇāṃ lohitāṅga ivoditaḥ
a tatas taṃ bhīmadhanvānaṃ kruddhāḥ sarve niśācarāḥ
c rāmaṃ nānāvidhaiḥ śastrair abhyavarṣanta durjayam
a mudgarair āyasaiḥ śūlaiḥ prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
c rākṣasāḥ samare rāmaṃ nijaghnū roṣatatparāḥ
a te balāhakasaṃkāśā mahānādā mahābalāḥ
c abhyadhāvanta kākutsthaṃ rāmaṃ yuddhe jighāṃsavaḥ
a te rāme śaravarṣāṇi vyasṛjan rakṣasāṃ guṇāḥ
c śailendram iva dhārābhir varṣamāṇā mahādhanāḥ
a sa taiḥ parivṛto ghorai rāghavo rakṣasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
c tithiṣv iva mahādevo vṛtaḥ pāriṣadāṃ gaṇaiḥ
a tāni muktāni śastrāṇi yātudhānaiḥ sa rāghavaḥ
c pratijagrāha viśikhair nadyoghān iva sāgaraḥ
a sa taiḥ praharaṇair ghorair bhinnagātro na vivyathe
c rāmaḥ pradīptair bahubhir vajrair iva mahācalaḥ
a sa viddhaḥ kṣatajādigdhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rāghavaḥ
c babhūva rāmaḥ saṃdhyābhrair divākara ivāvṛtaḥ
a viṣedur devagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
c ekaṃ sahastrair bahubhis tadā dṛṣṭvā samāvṛtam
a tato rāmaḥ susaṃkruddho maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ
c sasarja niśitān bāṇāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a durāvārān durviṣahān kālapāśopamān raṇe
c mumoca līlayā rāmaḥ kaṅkapatrān ajihmagān
a te śarāḥ śatrusainyeṣu muktā rāmeṇa līlayā
c ādadū rakṣasāṃ prāṇān pāśāḥ kālakṛtā iva
a bhittvā rākṣasadehāṃs tāṃs te śarā rudhirāplutāḥ
c antarikṣagatā rejur dīptāgnisamatejasaḥ
a asaṃkhyeyās tu rāmasya sāyakāś cāpamaṇḍalāt
c viniṣpetur atīvogrā rakṣaḥ prāṇāpahāriṇaḥ
a tair dhanūṃṣi dhvajāgrāṇi varmāṇi ca śirāṃsi ca
c bahūn sahastābharaṇān ūrūn karikaropamān
a tato nālīkanārācais tīkṣṇāgraiś ca vikarṇibhiḥ
c bhīmam ārtasvaraṃ cakrur bhidyamānā niśācarāḥ
a tat sainyaṃ niśitair bāṇair arditaṃ marmabhedibhiḥ
c rāmeṇa na sukhaṃ lebhe śuṣkaṃ vanam ivāgninā
a ke cid bhīmabalāḥ śūrāḥ śūlān khaḍgān paraśvadhān
c cikṣipuḥ paramakruddhā rāmāya rajanīcarāḥ
a tāni bāṇair mahābāhuḥ śastrāṇy āvārya rāghavaḥ
c jahāra samare prāṇāṃś ciccheda ca śirodharān
a avaśiṣṭāś ca ye tatra viṣaṇṇāś ca niśācarāḥ
c kharam evābhyadhāvanta śaraṇārthaṃ śarārditāḥ
a tān sarvān punar ādāya samāśvāsya ca dūṣaṇaḥ
c abhyadhāvata kākutsthaṃ kruddho rudram ivāntakaḥ
a nivṛttās tu punaḥ sarve dūṣaṇāśrayanirbhayāḥ
c rāmam evābhyadhāvanta sālatālaśilāyudhāḥ
a tad babhūvādbhutaṃ yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ romaharṣaṇam
c rāmasyāsya mahāghoraṃ punas teṣāṃ ca rakṣasām
a tad drumāṇāṃ śilānāṃ ca varṣaṃ prāṇaharaṃ mahat
c pratijagrāha dharmātmā rāghavas tīkṣṇasāyakaiḥ
a pratigṛhya ca tad varaṃ nimīlita ivarṣabhaḥ
c rāmaḥ krodhaṃ paraṃ bheje vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasām
a tataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭaḥ pradīpta iva tejasā
c śarair abhyakirat sainyaṃ sarvataḥ sahadūṣaṇam
a tataḥ senāpatiḥ kruddho dūṣaṇaḥ śatrudūṣaṇaḥ
c jagrāha giriśṛṅgābhaṃ parighaṃ romaharṣaṇam
a veṣṭitaṃ kāñcanaiḥ paṭṭair devasainyābhimardanam
c āyasaiḥ śaṅkubhis tīkṣṇaiḥ kīrṇaṃ paravasokṣitām
a vajrāśanisamasparśaṃ paragopuradāraṇam
c taṃ mahoragasaṃkāśaṃ pragṛhya parighaṃ raṇe
e dūṣaṇo 'bhyapatad rāmaṃ krūrakarmā niśācaraḥ
a tasyābhipatamānasya dūṣaṇasya sa rāghavaḥ
c dvābhyāṃ śarābhyāṃ ciccheda sahastābharaṇau bhujau
a bhraṣṭas tasya mahākāyaḥ papāta raṇamūrdhani
c parighaś chinnahastasya śakradhvaja ivāgrataḥ
a sa karābhyāṃ vikīrṇābhyāṃ papāta bhuvi dūṣaṇaḥ
c viṣāṇābhyāṃ viśīrṇābhyāṃ manasvīva mahāgajaḥ
a dṛṣṭvā taṃ patitaṃ bhūmau dūṣaṇaṃ nihataṃ raṇe
c sādhu sādhv iti kākutsthaṃ sarvabhūtāny apūjayan
a etasminn antare kruddhās trayaḥ senāgrayāyinaḥ
c saṃhatyābhyadravan rāmaṃ mṛtyupāśāvapāśitāḥ
e mahākapālaḥ sthūlākṣaḥ pramāthī ca mahābalaḥ
a mahākapālo vipulaṃ śūlam udyamya rākṣasaḥ
c sthūlākṣaḥ paṭṭiśaṃ gṛhya pramāthī ca paraśvadham
a dṛṣṭvaivāpatatas tāṃs tu rāghavaḥ sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ
c tīkṣṇāgraiḥ pratijagrāha saṃprāptān atithīn iva
a mahākapālasya śiraś ciccheda raghunaṅganaḥ
c asaṃkhyeyais tu bāṇaughaiḥ pramamātha pramāthinam
a sthūlākṣasyākṣiṇī tīkṣṇaiḥ pūrayām āsa sāyakaiḥ
c sa papāta hato bhūmau viṭapīva mahādrumaḥ
a tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśair hemavajravibhūṣitaiḥ
c jaghanaśeṣaṃ tejasvī tasya sainyasya sāyakaiḥ
a te rukmapuṅkhā viśikhāḥ sadhūmā iva pāvakāḥ
c nijaghnus tāni rakṣāṃsi vajrā iva mahādrumān
a rakṣasāṃ tu śataṃ rāmaḥ śatenaikena karṇinā
c sahasraṃ ca sahasreṇa jaghāna raṇamūrdhani
a tair bhinnavarmābharaṇāś chinnabhinnaśarāsanāḥ
c nipetuḥ śoṇitādigdhā dharaṇyāṃ rajanīcarāḥ
a tair muktakeśaiḥ samare patitaiḥ śoṇitokṣitaiḥ
c āstīrṇā vasudhā kṛtsnā mahāvediḥ kuśair iva
a kṣaṇena tu mahāghoraṃ vanaṃ nihatarākṣasaṃ
c babhūva niraya prakhyaṃ māṃsaśoṇitakardamam
a caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām
c hatāny ekena rāmeṇa mānuṣeṇa padātinā
a tasya sainyasya sarvasya kharaḥ śeṣo mahārathaḥ
c rākṣasas triśirāś caiva rāmaś ca ripusūdanaḥ
a tatas tu tad bhīmabalaṃ mahāhave
samīkṣya rāmeṇa hataṃ balīyasā
c rathena rāmaṃ mahatā kharas tataḥ
samāsasādendra ivodyatāśaniḥ
a kharaṃ tu rāmābhimukhaṃ prayāntaṃ vāhinīpatiḥ
c rākṣasas triśirā nāma saṃnipatyedam abravīt
a māṃ niyojaya vikrānta saṃnivartasva sāhasāt
c paśya rāmaṃ mahābāhuṃ saṃyuge vinipātitam
a pratijānāmi te satyam āyudhaṃ cāham ālabhe
c yathā rāmaṃ vadhiṣyāmi vadhārhaṃ sarvarakṣasām
a ahaṃ vāsya raṇe mṛtyur eṣa vā samare mama
c vinivartya raṇotsāhaṃ muhūrtaṃ prāśniko bhava
a prahṛṣṭo vā hate rāme janasthānaṃ prayāsyasi
c mayi vā nihate rāmaṃ saṃyugāyopayāsyasi
a kharas triśirasā tena mṛtyulobhāt prasāditaḥ
c gaccha yudhyety anujñāto rāghavābhimukho yayau
a triśirāś ca rathenaiva vājiyuktena bhāsvatā
c abhyadravad raṇe rāmaṃ triśṛṅga iva parvataḥ
a śaradhārā samūhān sa mahāmegha ivotsṛjan
c vyasṛjat sadṛśaṃ nādaṃ jalārdrasyeva dundubheḥ
a āgacchantaṃ triśirasaṃ rākṣasaṃ prekṣya rāghavaḥ
c dhanuṣā pratijagrāha vidhunvan sāyakāñ śitān
a sa saṃprahāras tumulo rāma triśirasor mahān
c babhūvātīva balinoḥ siṃhakuñjarayor iva
a tatas triśirasā bāṇair lalāṭe tāḍitas tribhiḥ
c amarṣī kupito rāmaḥ saṃrabdham idam abravīt
a aho vikramaśūrasya rākṣasasyedṛśaṃ balam
c puṣpair iva śarair yasya lalāṭe 'smi parikṣataḥ
e mamāpi pratigṛhṇīṣva śarāṃś cāpaguṇacyutān
a evam uktvā tu saṃrabdhaḥ śarān āśīviṣopamān
c triśiro vakṣasi kruddho nijaghāna caturdaśa
a caturbhis turagān asya śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c nyapātayata tejasvī caturas tasya vājinaḥ
a aṣṭabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ sūtaṃ rathopasthe nyapātayat
c rāmaś ciccheda bāṇena dhvajaṃ cāsya samucchritam
a tato hatarathāt tasmād utpatantaṃ niśācaram
c bibheda rāmas taṃ bāṇair hṛdaye so 'bhavaj jaḍaḥ
a sāyakaiś cāprameyātmā sāmarṣas tasya rakṣasaḥ
c śirāṃsy apātayat trīṇi vegavadbhis tribhiḥ śataiḥ
a sa bhūmau śoṇitodgārī rāmabāṇābhipīḍitaḥ
c nyapatat patitaiḥ pūrvaṃ svaśirobhir niśācaraḥ
a hataśeṣās tato bhagnā rākṣasāḥ kharasaṃśrayāḥ
c dravanti sma na tiṣṭhanti vyāghratrastā mṛgā iva
a tān kharo dravato dṛṣṭvā nivartya ruṣitaḥ svayam
c rāmam evābhidudrāva rāhuś candramasaṃ yathā
a nihataṃ dūṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā raṇe triśirasā saha
c kharasyāpy abhavat trāso dṛṣṭvā rāmasya vikramam
a sa dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ sainyam aviṣahyaṃ mahābalam
c hatam ekena rāmeṇa dūṣaṇas triśirā api
a tad balaṃ hatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vimanāḥ prekṣya rākṣasaḥ
c āsasāda kharo rāmaṃ namucir vāsavaṃ yathā
a vikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ nārācān raktabhojanān
c kharaś cikṣepa rāmāya kruddhān āśīviṣān iva
a jyāṃ vidhunvan subahuśaḥ śikṣayāstrāṇi darśayan
c cacāra samare mārgāñ śarai rathagataḥ kharaḥ
a sa sarvāś ca diśo bāṇaiḥ pradiśaś ca mahārathaḥ
c pūrayām āsa taṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmo 'pi sumahad dhanuḥ
a sa sāyakair durviṣahaiḥ sasphuliṅgair ivāgnibhiḥ
c nabhaś cakārāvivaraṃ parjanya iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ
a tad babhūva śitair bāṇaiḥ khararāmavisarjitaiḥ
c paryākāśam anākāśaṃ sarvataḥ śarasaṃkulam
a śarajālāvṛtaḥ sūryo na tadā sma prakāśate
c anyonyavadhasaṃrambhād ubhayoḥ saṃprayudhyatoḥ
a tato nālīkanārācais tīkṣṇāgraiś ca vikarṇibhiḥ
c ājaghāna raṇe rāmaṃ totrair iva mahādvipam
a taṃ rathasthaṃ dhanuṣpāṇiṃ rākṣasaṃ paryavasthitam
c dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni pāśahastam ivāntakam
a taṃ siṃham iva vikrāntaṃ siṃhavikrāntagāminam
c dṛṣṭvā nodvijate rāmaḥ siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā
a tataḥ sūryanikāśena rathena mahatā kharaḥ
c āsasāda raṇe rāmaṃ pataṅga iva pāvakam
a tato 'sya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ muṣṭideśe mahātmanaḥ
c kharaś ciccheda rāmasya darśayan pāṇilāghavam
a sa punas tv aparān sapta śarān ādāya varmaṇi
c nijaghāna raṇe kruddhaḥ śakrāśanisamaprabhān
a tatas tat prahataṃ bāṇaiḥ kharamuktaiḥ suparvabhiḥ
c papāta kavacaṃ bhūmau rāmasyādityavarcasaḥ
a sa śarair arpitaḥ kruddhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rāghavaḥ
c rarāja samare rāmo vidhūmo 'gnir iva jvalan
a tato gambhīranirhrādaṃ rāmaḥ śatrunibarhaṇaḥ
c cakārāntāya sa ripoḥ sajyam anyan mahad dhanuḥ
a sumahad vaiṣṇavaṃ yat tad atisṛṣṭaṃ maharṣiṇā
c varaṃ tad dhanur udyamya kharaṃ samabhidhāvata
a tataḥ kanakapuṅkhais tu śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
c ciccheda rāmaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kharasya samare dhvajam
a sa darśanīyo bahudhā vicchinnaḥ kāñcano dhvajaḥ
c jagāma dharaṇīṃ sūryo devatānām ivājñayā
a taṃ caturbhiḥ kharaḥ kruddho rāmaṃ gātreṣu mārgaṇaiḥ
c vivyādha hṛdi marmajño mātaṅgam iva tomaraiḥ
a sa rāmo bahubhir bāṇaiḥ kharakārmukaniḥsṛtaiḥ
c viddho rudhirasiktāṅgo babhūva ruṣito bhṛśam
a sa dhanur dhanvināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pragṛhya paramāhave
c mumoca parameṣvāsaḥ ṣaṭ śarān abhilakṣitān
a śirasy ekena bāṇena dvābhyāṃ bāhvor athārpayat
c tribhiś candrārdhavaktraiś ca vakṣasy abhijaghāna ha
a tataḥ paścān mahātejā nārācān bhāskaropamān
c jighāṃsū rākṣasaṃ kruddhas trayodaśa śilāśitān
a tato 'sya yugam ekena caturbhiś caturo hayān
c ṣaṣṭhena ca śiraḥ saṃkhye ciccheda kharasāratheḥ
a tribhis triveṇuṃ balavān dvābhyām akṣaṃ mahābalaḥ
c dvādaśena tu bāṇena kharasya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ
e chittvā vajranikāśena rāghavaḥ prahasann iva
g trayodaśenendrasamo bibheda samare kharam
a prabhagnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ
c gadāpāṇir avaplutya tasthau bhūmau kharas tadā
a tat karma rāmasya mahārathasya
sametya devāś ca maharṣayaś ca
c apūjayan prāñjalayaḥ prahṛṣṭās
tadā vimānāgragatāḥ sametāḥ
a kharaṃ tu virathaṃ rāmo gadāpāṇim avasthitam
c mṛdupūrvaṃ mahātejāḥ paruṣaṃ vākyam abravīt
a gajāśvarathasaṃbādhe bale mahati tiṣṭhatā
c kṛtaṃ sudāruṇaṃ karma sarvalokajugupsitam
a udvejanīyo bhūtānāṃ nṛśaṃsaḥ pāpakarmakṛt
c trayāṇām api lokānām īśvaro 'pi na tiṣṭhati
a karma lokaviruddhaṃ tu kurvāṇaṃ kṣaṇadācara
c tīkṣṇaṃ sarvajano hanti sarpaṃ duṣṭam ivāgatam
a lobhāt pāpāni kurvāṇaḥ kāmād vā yo na budhyate
c bhraṣṭaḥ paśyati tasyāntaṃ brāhmaṇī karakād iva
a vasato daṇḍakāraṇye tāpasān dharmacāriṇaḥ
c kiṃ nu hatvā mahābhāgān phalaṃ prāpsyasi rākṣasa
a na ciraṃ pāpakarmāṇaḥ krūrā lokajugupsitāḥ
c aiśvaryaṃ prāpya tiṣṭhanti śīrṇamūlā iva drumāḥ
a avaśyaṃ labhate kartā phalaṃ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ
c ghoraṃ paryāgate kāle drumaḥ puṣpam ivārtavam
a nacirāt prāpyate loke pāpānāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalam
c saviṣāṇām ivānnānāṃ bhuktānāṃ kṣaṇadācara
a pāpam āccaratāṃ ghoraṃ lokasyāpriyam icchatām
c aham āsādito rājā prāṇān hantuṃ niśācara
a adya hi tvāṃ mayā muktāḥ śarāḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇāḥ
c vidārya nipatiṣyanti valmīkam iva pannagāḥ
a ye tvayā daṇḍakāraṇye bhakṣitā dharmacāriṇaḥ
c tān adya nihataḥ saṃkhye sasainyo 'nugamiṣyasi
a adya tvāṃ nihataṃ bāṇaiḥ paśyantu paramarṣayaḥ
c nirayasthaṃ vimānasthā ye tvayā hiṃsitāḥ purā
a prahara tvaṃ yathākāmaṃ kuru yatnaṃ kulādhama
c adya te pātayiṣyāmi śiras tālaphalaṃ yathā
a evam uktas tu rāmeṇa kruddhaḥ saṃraktalocanaḥ
c pratyuvāca tato rāmaṃ prahasan krodhamūrchitaḥ
a prākṛtān rākṣasān hatvā yuddhe daśarathātmaja
c ātmanā katham ātmānam apraśasyaṃ praśaṃsasi
a vikrāntā balavanto vā ye bhavanti nararṣabhāḥ
c kathayanti na te kiṃ cit tejasā svena garvitāḥ
a prākṛtās tv akṛtātmāno loke kṣatriyapāṃsanāḥ
c nirarthakaṃ vikatthante yathā rāma vikatthase
a kulaṃ vyapadiśan vīraḥ samare ko 'bhidhāsyati
c mṛtyukāle hi saṃprāpte svayam aprastave stavam
a sarvathā tu laghutvaṃ te katthanena vidarśitam
c suvarṇapratirūpeṇa tapteneva kuśāgninā
a na tu mām iha tiṣṭhantaṃ paśyasi tvaṃ gadādharam
c dharādharam ivākampyaṃ parvataṃ dhātubhiś citam
a paryāpto 'haṃ gadāpāṇir hantuṃ prāṇān raṇe tava
c trayāṇām api lokānāṃ pāśahasta ivāntakaḥ
a kāmaṃ bahv api vaktavyaṃ tvayi vakṣyāmi na tv aham
c astaṃ gacched dhi savitā yuddhavighras tato bhavet
a caturdaśa sahasrāṇi rākṣasānāṃ hatāni te
c tvadvināśāt karomy adya teṣām aśrupramārjanam
a ity uktvā paramakruddhas tāṃ gadāṃ paramāṅgadām
c kharaś cikṣepa rāmāya pradīptām aśaniṃ yathā
a kharabāhupramuktā sā pradīptā mahatī gadā
c bhasmavṛkṣāṃś ca gulmāṃś ca kṛtvāgāt tatsamīpataḥ
a tām āpatantīṃ jvalitāṃ mṛtyupāśopamāṃ gadā
c antarikṣagatāṃ rāmaś ciccheda bahudhā śaraiḥ
a sā viśīrṇā śarair bhinnā papāta dharaṇītale
c gadāmantrauṣadhibalair vyālīva vinipātitā
a bhittvā tu tāṃ gadāṃ bāṇai rāghavo dharmavatsalaḥ
c smayamānaḥ kharaṃ vākyaṃ saṃrabdham idam abravīt
a etat te balasarvasvaṃ darśitaṃ rākṣasādhama
c śaktihīnataro matto vṛthā tvam upagarjitam
a eṣā bāṇavinirbhinnā gadā bhūmitalaṃ gatā
c abhidhānapragalbhasya tava pratyayaghātinī
a yat tvayoktaṃ vinaṣṭānām idam aśrupramārjanam
c rākṣasānāṃ karomīti mithyā tad api te vacaḥ
a nīcasya kṣudraśīlasya mithyāvṛttasya rakṣasaḥ
c prāṇān apahariṣyāmi garutmān amṛtaṃ yathā
a adya te bhinnakaṇṭhasya phenabudbudabhūṣitam
c vidāritasya madbāṇair mahī pāsyati śoṇitam
a pāṃsurūṣitasarvāṅgaḥ srastanyastabhujadvayaḥ
c svapsyase gāṃ samāśliṣya durlabhāṃ pramadām iva
a pravṛddhanidre śayite tvayi rākṣasapāṃsane
c bhaviṣyanty aśaraṇyānāṃ śaraṇyā daṇḍakā ime
a janasthāne hatasthāne tava rākṣasamaccharaiḥ
c nirbhayā vicariṣyanti sarvato munayo vane
a adya viprasariṣyanti rākṣasyo hatabāndhavāḥ
c bāṣpārdravadanā dīnā bhayād anyabhayāvahāḥ
a adya śokarasajñās tā bhaviṣyanti niśācara
c anurūpakulāḥ patnyo yāsāṃ tvaṃ patir īdṛśaḥ
a nṛśaṃsaśīla kṣudrātman nityaṃ brāhmaṇakaṇṭaka
c tvatkṛte śaṅkitair agnau munibhiḥ pātyate haviḥ
a tam evam abhisaṃrabdhaṃ bruvāṇaṃ rāghavaṃ raṇe
c kharo nirbhartsayām āsa roṣāt kharatara svanaḥ
